Chapter 2901: I didn’t expect you to be like this, Senior Song!

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Golden Trigram’s memories had been ‘sealed’ before, and he knew this very well—because he didn’t have any memories before he joined the Heavenly Court!

Not long ago, when he was inheriting the position of the Heavenly Emperor, the Heavenly Emperor had personally answered his doubts about sealing his memories. According to the Celestial Thearch, he was once a disciple that the Celestial Thearch had secretly taken in before establishing the celestial heavens. His cultivation techniques, knowledge, and methods were all taught by the Heavenly Emperor. This was also the reason why he was unable to take the final step on the path to immortality. This was because his path was actually the path of the Heavenly Emperor! Under the premise that the Celestial Thearch had a master, he could not attain immortality.

According to the Heavenly Emperor’s explanation, the reason for sealing his memories was to prevent him from being involved in the disaster during the process of building the Heavenly Court. Later, after the Heavenly Court was successfully established, the Celestial Thearch brought him into the Heavenly Court. However, he brought him into the Heavenly Court as a ‘newbie’ and built his own celestial palace for him. The Celestial Thearch’s explanation was generally reasonable and there was nothing to doubt.

However, after the Heavenly Emperor passed the Heavenly Emperor’s seat to him, he still did not undo the seal on his memory. Back then, it was because the Heavenly Emperor had used the topic of ‘Senior Song’ to divert his attention, causing him to forget about the matter of the ‘memory seal’.

And now... Just as Island Master Golden Trigram turned around and glanced at Song Shuhang, the memories in Golden Trigram’s mind began to surface with the help of the ‘laws of time’, ‘the path of the Heavenly City’, ‘Tyrannical Song’s special physique’, and other factors.

He discovered that the first time he met Song Shuhang wasn’t on the mysterious island.

“The Ghost God Fragment was originally a female. However, after my modification, I naturally had to change the settings and turn the female into a male... Hmm, Heavenly Emperor. From today onwards, you are the Heavenly Emperor!” A mechanical voice sounded.

However, at this moment, Golden Trigram found that his vision was completely dark. And then... The ‘image’ he saw jumped. This was because the scene he was seeing now was centered around ‘Song Shuhang’. It was the memories related to Song Shuhang that had been extracted.

In his memory, Golden Trigram found that he was a boy around six years old.

“Is this how I looked like when I was young? Is it my childhood memory?” Golden Trigram was moved. “Could it be that I came into contact with ‘Tyrannical Song’ when I was six years old?”

“Could it be... The Celestial Thearch didn’t trick me. Is she telling the truth? The one who is really lying is Tyrannical Song?!”

But why would Tyrannical Song lie? Many thoughts flashed through Golden Trigram’s mind.

As his thoughts raced, the scenes in his memory slowly unfolded. In his memory, a strange person with ‘dual-pupils’ appeared. He began to teach the six-year-old Golden Trigram about cultivation and assisted him in his cultivation. The cultivation method taught by the strange man was extremely compatible with the young Golden Trigram. It was as if it was tailor-made for him.

“Could this strange person be the Heavenly Emperor? Was it her incarnation? Is she teaching me how to cultivate?” Golden Trigram guessed after combining it with the explanation given by the Heavenly Emperor. Because it was a memory, the images flashed through his mind very quickly.

In any case, he cultivated day and night and ate pills... Then, there was the scene of day cultivation, night cultivation, and eating pills. In just four short years, he had advanced to the Fourth Stage Realm! If this cultivation speed was placed in the myriad worlds, it would be so fast that it was terrifying!

In the next five years, he condensed a Supreme Golden Core with nine dragon patterns and advanced to the Fifth Stage! His cultivation was extremely smooth!

“Strange, where’s Tyrannical Song?” Island Master Golden Trigram asked curiously.

Since the memory was centered around Song Shuhang, it meant that Song Shuhang had always been by his side in this scene. However, ever since he started cultivating at the age of six, he hadn’t found any trace of Tyrannical Song.

“Wait, could it be... This weirdo with dual-pupils is Tyrannical Song?”

Because in the picture, there was only the young him and the strange man with dual-pupils!

“If this weirdo with dual-pupils is Tyrannical Song, then he is indeed my ‘senior’... However, the Celestial Thearch’s words were suspicious. Isn’t she the one who accepted me as her disciple? Tyrannical Song or Heavenly Emperor, who is lying?” Golden Trigram frowned and continued reading. As long as his memories were fully unfolded, the truth would be revealed!

The scene was still progressing slowly. After reaching the Fifth Stage Realm, the strange man with dual-pupils left. He left... He left just like that!

However, the scene of the memory still hadn’t ended. The memory with Song Shuhang as the center was still unfolding!

“Isn’t the dual-pupiled freak Tyrannical Song? And Tyrannical Song is still hidden in my memories? Where is he?” Island Master Golden Trigram was completely confused. His memories were still progressing rapidly...

The young him quickly entered the segment of the Golden Core composition. The Golden Core Formation was not a problem for him. He used the nine dragon patterns as ink to construct a Golden Core Heavenly City Formation!

“It’s indeed the path of the Heavenly Court... When I was at the Fifth Stage Spiritual Emperor Realm, my path was already set. The Celestial Thearch did not lie about this.”

The progress of the Golden Core composition was very fast. It did not take long for it to reach 99%. Now, it was only missing the finishing touch! For cultivators of the cultivation system, the finishing touch of the Golden Core was extremely important. A golden core determined the great path, and this finishing touch was the most important part of the golden core.

The young man’s smooth cultivation finally met a bottleneck. He was stuck in the ‘Finishing Eye’. This stroke required an epiphany.

“Tyrannical Song still hasn’t appeared,” Golden Trigram frowned. “So, where was Tyrannical Song?”

Just as Golden Trigram was feeling puzzled... The young man in the picture made a shocking move.

“Right, at this time, you can pray to ‘God’!” the youth said.

Golden Trigram was dumbfounded.

“What the hell was praying to God? This can’t be me! I can’t be this funny!” But the young man in his memory had taken action. He began to build an altar and prayed seriously, “God, I pray to you here. Please guide me in the next direction. It’s best if it’s close to me, because if it’s too far, I won’t be able to find the direction.”

Then, it was the process of the young man praying seriously. What shocked Golden Trigram was that the young man seemed to have received feedback from a certain voice. As the young man continued to ask questions, a clear sentence finally appeared in Golden Trigram’s ears.

“Courting death is a virus called Thrice Reckless Disease. It was terrifyingly contagious. If you really want to try to court death, then go to the highest mountain peak, seal your spiritual qi, and jump down with all your might. Leap of Faith. During the process of landing, you will experience the feeling of ‘death’ approaching.”

Golden Trigram:

Then, the young man in his memory happily ran to the highest peak—he came to the cliff where he would definitely be crushed if he jumped down. Then, he began to seriously seal his spiritual power.

“No, don’t be so stupid!” Golden Trigram shouted. He was about to cry from this youth’s stupidity.

“None of this is a problem!” The young man shouted and jumped into the cliff under Golden Trigram’s desperate gaze!

“Is this the feeling of death?” the young man asked excitedly as he jumped down. “Something in my body seems to have awakened. I feel like I can enter the last stroke of the Golden Core composition. It’s time to stop.”

“Not good, I don’t know how to stop!”

Other than cultivating, the young man had never refined a magic weapon... Moreover, he had sealed his spiritual energy.

Hong

As Golden Trigram’s stomach ached, the young man’s body smashed into the ground, creating a huge pit. He was covered in blood and spat out large mouthfuls of blood. He was trembling as he tried to get up... However, after only two steps, the young man fainted.

The memory ended.

“It’s you, Senior Song!” Golden Trigram stared at Song Shuhang. The voice that tricked him into sealing his spiritual energy and jumping off the cliff was Tyrannical Song!

Chapter 2902: So, It Is!

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Even now, Golden Trigram hadn’t figured out what he experienced when he was young. He didn’t know who his parents were or how he was born. After all, in his memory, when the plot started, he was already six years old.

However, he was certain that the voice that had tricked him into jumping off the cliff in his memory was the voice of ‘Tyrannical Song’!

The Heavenly Emperor was right about Senior Song.

Tyrannical Song had existed since ancient times!

In ancient times, when he was still young and ignorant, Tyrannical Song had always been by his side in a mysterious and undetectable way.

It was the real Senior Song.

Opposite him, Song Shuhang was dumbfounded.

The effect of the ‘scene backtracking’ of the Dao of Time was mutual. When Island Master Golden Trigram opened his memories, Song Shuhang could also receive the scene of this part.

“Senior Song!” Island Master Golden Trigram tightly hugged the rabbit in his arms and stared at Song Shuhang.

“Wait... why do you have this memory?” Song Shuhang rubbed the space between his eyebrows and stretched out his palm toward Golden Trigram, indicating for him to pause.

This person didn’t match up with his memories.

Shouldn’t this memory about his ‘dream’ be targeted at the Heavenly Emperor?

Why did the Island Master, Senior Golden Trigram, also have this memory?

“Shouldn’t I be the one asking you this question, Senior Song?” Island Lord Golden Trigram said slowly, his voice carrying a hint of resentment.

In his memories, he was a cute and stupid boy when he was young, but Senior Song actually cruelly tricked him into jumping off the cliff!

Was this something humans did?

As he spoke, Immortal Fairy White Bones, Zither Master Fengyi, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, Senior Turtle, and the others all recovered from their ‘Scene Rewind’ state.

The memories of their encounter with Song Shuhang were very normal, and there were no surprises.

After leaving the influence of the ‘Dao of Time,’ they looked at Song Shuhang and Golden Trigram in confusion. Why did Golden Trigram suddenly change his mind and call Song Shuhang ‘Senior Song’?

Next, Pavilion Master Chu’s hair regained its vitality.

Afterward, Senior White and Soft Feather also recovered.

“There’s something wrong with this memory...because it is the memory of Heavenly Emperor Da Da Zi,” Song Shuhang said to Golden Trigram.

“Are you sure?” Golden Trigram was stunned.

“Yes, I’m sure,” Song Shuhang said.

The conditions to activate his dreamland talent were also traceable. At the very least, before entering the dream, he would have a certain degree of ‘contact’ with the person in the dream.

Whether it was blood contact, soul contact, or law contact... In short, there would always be an opportunity to come into contact before the dreamland talent took effect.

At that time, when he was dreaming of the young Heavenly Emperor, Song Shuhang only had the opportunity to enter the dream with Heavenly Emperor Zi. It had nothing to do with the Island Master Golden Trigram.

But now...under the influence of the Dao of Time, Island Master Golden Trigram suddenly controlled this part of his memory.

“So, Golden Trigram, what is the secret between you and Tyrannical Song?” Immortal Fairy White Bones’ interest in gossip was piqued, and she asked curiously.

Golden Trigram ignored White Bones Immortal Fairy’s gossiping and guessed, “Could it be that I inherited the Dao of Heavenly Emperor, so I inherited a part of her karma?”

“It’s possible,” Song Shuhang said.

At the same time, he carefully recalled the memories of the young Heavenly Emperor who had entered his dream.

He had once thought that the memories of the young Heavenly Emperor that he had dreamt of might have a continuation. In the end, even now that the Heavenly Emperor had died, there was still no clue as to what to do with the sequels.

Now, even if he entered the dream again, it wouldn’t be of much help to Song Shuhang.

After carefully recalling, Song Shuhang still found a few interesting points.

There were a few important details in the dream.

The Heavenly Emperor’s original form was a fragment of the ‘Ghost God Cheng Lin,’ and she should be in a female form. However, after the manipulation of the Heavenly Dao Ball’s big boss, he turned from a female into a male and fiddled with the young Heavenly Emperor.

In addition, there was a six-year blank period in the memories of the young Heavenly Emperor. It was the period of the young Heavenly Emperor from infancy to the age of six. When Song Shuhang entered the dream, this period of memory was skipped.

But... Song Shuhang had a vague feeling that the young Heavenly Emperor before the age of six had already sensed ‘his’ existence.

Later on, when the young Heavenly Emperor encountered a difficult problem, the first thing he thought of was the option of praying to God.

After the young Heavenly Emperor turned six years old, no one had ever mentioned the existence of a ‘god’ to him. No one had ever mentioned the operation of praying to a god to him.

Therefore, the answer was very likely to be in the six years of memory that had disappeared.

In addition, according to the information that Song Shuhang had obtained after coming into contact with the Heavenly Emperor, it could be verified with the memories of the dream.

After the Heavenly Emperor had officially occupied Soft Feather’s ghost spirit, he had been in his female form.

According to the memories of the White Dragon and the others, the ‘Celestial Emperor’ of the ancient Heavenly City was in a male form.

The Celestial Thearch herself had mentioned that her origin was female. Therefore, the resurrected Celestial Thearch should have been restored from the fat ball’s method of turning a female into a male.

Combining the clues and deducing, the identity of the Island Master Golden Trigram was intriguing.

“Speaking of which...can the path to immortality be inherited by others?” Song Shuhang suddenly said.

“It can’t be,” Immortal Fairy White Bones said.

“The path to immortality is the comprehension and sublimation of one’s own path. There are no two identical leaves in this world, and it’s the same for life. Different experiences would lead to different Daos. Thus, no one’s Dao can completely fit with another’s,” Pavilion Master Chu said thoughtfully.

She suddenly thought of Fairy Cheng Lin and Slow-Witted Song.

Slow-Witted Song had personally mentioned to her that he had mastered Cheng Lin’s path to immortality and the path to nurturing new life.

“The Celestial Thearch said that the path of the celestial heavens is very special. Therefore, it can be inherited to other people in the celestial heavens like inheriting the throne,” said Island Lord Golden Trigram.

“Then, can you pass the path of the Heavenly Emperor to me? It can’t be, right?” Song Shuhang was like a detective who had found the truth. “So, why did the Heavenly Emperor inherit the path to immortality for you?”

“You’re not a member of the ancient Heavenly City,” Pavilion Master Chu said in a daze.

“Cough, but the path of the Heavenly Emperor can’t be inherited by others, right? For example, I can’t inherit it to Fairy Virtue?” Song Shuhang pulled Fairy? out.

Island Master Golden Trigram said, “It seems that it can’t.”

“So, Senior Island Master, have you ever thought that actually... you’re the Heavenly Emperor!” Song Shuhang finally voiced out his guess.

Island Master Golden Trigram was speechless.

“If this is the case, everything makes sense. You and the Celestial Thearch will have the same childhood experience. You will lose your memories, but you will be able to perfectly inherit the Celestial Thearch’s Dao without any rejection.” Song Shuhang shook his head and said, “There are no two identical leaves in the world, but a leaf can have two sides. Senior Island Master, you might be the other side of Tiandi Zi!”

Chapter 2903: Soft Feather and Senior White Are Coming Home for New Year’s

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Hearing this, Soft Feather’s eyes lit up. “So, Senior Island Master, are you going to jump up as well?”

Fairy Creation interjected, “Divination!”

“It’s really possible,” Song Shuhang nodded.

Island Master Golden Trigram: “???”

Why did the topic suddenly shift?

At the same time, he began to seriously consider Song Shuhang’s suggestion.

Could it be... Was he really the opposite side of the Celestial Thearch?

The more he thought about it, the more plausible it seemed.

“So, am I actually a fairy?” Island Master Golden Trigram asked after a long pause.

He was starting to doubt himself.

Because Senior Song’s deduction was reasonable, he couldn’t find a point to refute.

“To be honest, there’s no point in us guessing here. If Senior Island Master has the patience, you might as well wait for a while. When Da Da Zi is resurrected, you can get the answer from her no matter what questions you have,” Song Shuhang reminded.

“How much of her words do you think we can trust?” Island Master Golden Trigram sighed.

“That’s right... The more beautiful a woman is, the better she is at lying. Mother Zhang’s quote,” Song Shuhang nodded.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, are you saying that all the fairies here are liars?” Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet suddenly smiled.

Song Shuhang was dumbfounded

In an instant, he felt that the surrounding fairies were looking at him with unfriendly gazes.

This was a question of death.

A. “Fairy, you’re not liars.”

B. “Fairy, you’re all beautiful.”

If you choose A, do you mean that the fairies here are not beautiful?

Choosing B, are you saying that all the fairies here are dishonest and like to lie?

“Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet, are you a mental demon?” Song Shuhang said.

“No, I’m Tombstone,” replied Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet honestly.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

After the New Year, he had to think about which big shot he should go against next and make a list.

For example, the other incarnations of Void Sun in the universe?

Or the one who created the stellar destruction virus?

“Senior Song.” At this time, Island Lord Golden Trigram said in a deep voice.

“Senior Island Master, do you have any other questions?” Song Shuhang asked.

“No matter what happened in the past, Senior Song, I’ll think about how you induced me to jump off the cliff in ancient times when I get back,” said Island Lord Golden Trigram.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

The Island Master Senior holds a grudge.JPG

“At that time, I will welcome Senior Song to the mysterious island.” “Fellow Daoists, I’ll go first,” Island Lord Golden Trigram continued.

There were still people who were thinking about his mysterious island, so he had to be wary.

After the fairies and Golden Trigram returned the greeting and bade farewell, Island Master Golden Trigram hurriedly opened a spatial gate and left with Rabbit in his arms.

They came and went in a hurry.

After Island Master Golden Trigram left, Soft Feather curiously asked, “Ancient times? Senior Song, did you come into contact with Senior Island Master in ancient times?”

“No, I didn’t. I only inserted myself into the Celestial Thearch’s memories through some special method?” Song Shuhang tried to organize his words.

As his realm and vision increased, Song Shuhang became more and more aware of how unreasonable his talent in the Dreamland was.

Therefore, other than the pendant on his body and the seniors of the Nine Provinces Number One Group that he trusted, he didn’t want more people to know about his innate ability to enter the dream.

It was not that he was worried about what others would do to him. With his current combat strength, there were not many big shots in the myriad worlds who could press him to the ground.

It was purely to avoid unnecessary suspicion and trouble.

His ambiguous words made Zither Master Feng Yi, Immortal Fairy White Bones, and the other fairies even more confused.

Pavilion Master Chu’s hair curled up slightly, and she began to spin like a bamboo dragonfly.

Ye Si hugged Song Shuhang’s neck and floated in the air. Then, she would blow Pavilion Master Chu’s hair from time to time, making it spin faster.

“Is Fairy Chu thinking about something?” Immortal Fairy White Bones had been secretly paying attention to Pavilion Master Chu’s dazed state, so she asked.

“I’m too lazy to think, so I’m in the air. Don’t disturb me,” Pavilion Master Chu said lazily.

Immortal Fairy White Bones was confused.

“Shuhang, where are we going next?” Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword was full of energy as he asked.

“This matter is over. Next, I want to return to the main world, Earth. It’s the New Year,” Song Shuhang said. “I want to go home and take a look.”

It was also time to introduce his “daughter” to his parents. Song Shuhang looked at the mechanical girl in his hand, whose upper body had turned into a human shape, and whose lower body was still in the shape of a ball.

Then, he would spend the last peaceful New Year with his parents.

After saying this much, Song Shuhang looked at the few seniors beside him and said, “Seniors, what are your plans?”

After pondering for a moment, Zither Master Feng Yi flew to Song Shuhang’s shoulder and stopped. Her main body hadn’t been resurrected yet, and she had nowhere to go. Therefore, she wanted to move together with Song Shuhang.

“New Year? Bring me along!” Immortal Fairy White Bones replied. While Song Shuhang was killing the three corpses, she had vaguely sensed some information and wasn’t planning to leave for the time being.

“I have to follow you and get first-hand information about Lady Onion at any time,” Senior Turtle said worriedly.

“Senior Song, my father is still in seclusion on the World Tree. I don’t know if he will wake up during the New Year, so... I’ll go back to the modern world with you for the New Year,” Soft Feather raised her hand to sign up.

“Alright, Soft Feather, you guys follow me. I’ll bring everyone back to the main world in a while,” Song Shuhang said.

After saying that, he looked at Senior White.

“Oh.” Senior White came back to his senses and nodded. “After the New Year, I’ll have to shut myself up for a longer period of time. So, enjoy the New Year to your heart’s content.”

“Me too,” Song Shuhang nodded.

Perhaps this would be his last New Year.

Therefore, he had to be thick-skinned and ask for the most red packets this year.

Song Shuhang stretched out his hand and pressed in the air.

The spatial gate opened, and it was the coordinates leading to the vicinity of the world of the golden lotus.

The most convenient function of a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender was that they could save a lot of traveling time.

Not long after Song Shuhang and the others disappeared...

Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly and Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue rushed to the place where they had disappeared.

“Where is he?” Senior Spirit Butterfly looked at the empty place and the wooden blade stuck in the ground with a puzzled expression.

Where’s my daughter?

“I’ll ask in the group.” Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue opened the “cultivation chat” client and the “Nine Provinces Number Two Group.”

[Envious Senior Style] Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue: “Are Soft Feather and the others with you?”

“Eh? Senior Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue, you’re awake.” [Server. Cheng Goudan. Group Leader] Song Shuhang replied, “Soft Feather and I went home for the New Year.”

Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue was speechless.

He turned to look at Fellow Daoist Spirit Butterfly.

“Go back... Go home... New Year?” Lord Spirit Butterfly gradually lost his soul and became Lord Butterfly.

[Always-on Saint Seiya] Northern River’s Loose Cultivator saw the content of the chat and quickly added thoughtfully from afar, “Is Senior White with you, Shuhang?”

“Yes, Senior White also came home with me to celebrate the New Year,” Song Shuhang replied.

At the same time, Song Shuhang contacted the White Dragon through private chat, “Sister White Dragon, has Sixteen finished her seclusion?”

However... The White Dragon didn’t reply immediately.

[Mother Yellow Mountain·Group Owner] Venerable Yellow Mountain: “This year, there are more members online. It’s quite rare. How about... we get together during the New Year? It just so happens that I’ve already sent out the red packets that little friend Shuhang and I prepared for everyone.”

The members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group didn’t really care about the concept of “New Year” anymore.

After all, they were all cultivators.

At this time in the past, most of the members who were online were either cultivating in seclusion, refining pills in seclusion, or going out to search for treasures.

This year, the number of people who were awake online had reached a new high.

[CPU[Pluto] Young Master Phoenix Slayer said, “Then why don’t we... go to Shuhang’s place for the New Year?”

Chapter 2904: Quickly Withdraw, Don’t Give Shuhang a Chance to Show Off!

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

[Dog Food Medicine King] Medicine Master: “Going to Shuhang’s house for the New Year? Ziyan and I are fine with it. We are traveling everywhere now, so we can go anywhere. [Medicine Master + Riverly Purple Mist heart emoji] But where is Shuhang’s house now? Is he going to his hometown, Wenzhou City, for the New Year? Or should we go to the scholarly faction’s world of the golden lotus?”

Senior Medicine Master’s parents were still alive, but they had also lived for hundreds of years and were already indifferent to the concept of the New Year. In addition, Medicine Master and Riverly Purple Mist were still in their honeymoon period, so even during the traditional New Year, Medicine Master and Riverly Purple Mist would go out for a stroll. His parents would be secretly happy, wishing they would come back with two chubby babies.

[Steel Friend] Doudou: “Woof~ Medicine Master, even if I’m a dog, can you guys not force me to eat dog food? It’s too deliberate! The way you show off your affection is too deliberate! Woof, there are still kids in the group. Be careful!”

[The Man Who Likes Making Wishes] Palace Master Seven Lives Talisman: “How about we go to Wenzhou City for the New Year? I have a wish in my wish book to accompany the most important person to Wenzhou City to see the sea. Going to Wenzhou for the New Year is perfect to fulfill this wish. Damn it, I don’t even know when I made this wish! Damn it!”

[Cave Lord] Snow Wolf: “Manor Head, are you going to force us to eat dog food? That’s enough. It’s the New Year. Why must I eat your dog food? Isn’t my wolf food fragrant?”

Palace Master Seven Lives Talisman: “???”

When did I feed you guys dog food? You’re not my dog, so why should I feed you dog food?

[Gravitational Wave] Fairy Firefly: “Prefecture Master, which fairy is the most important person you want to accompany to Wenzhou to see the sea? Why haven’t we received any news?”

I haven’t heard of Palace Master Seven Lives Talisman dating any fairies recently.

Palace Master Seven Lives Talisman said, “The most important people I’m talking about are you guys! What are you thinking?”

[Master of Emoticons] Abbot Profound Principle: [thumbs up emoji]

It would be too difficult to rely on the ‘cultivation chat’ function to collect fees in the short term.

“Aren’t spirit stones the most basic thing in the cultivation world? I heard that when cultivating, you can’t do without spirit stones. Without spirit stones, how are you going to cultivate? Didn’t you save some?” Papa Song was puzzled.

After staying in the scholarly faction for a few days, Papa Song had gained some basic knowledge about the cultivation world, such as medicinal pills and spirit stones. Every cultivator couldn’t leave them when they were in seclusion.

It was common to see scholarly disciples using spirit stones to absorb spirit energy.

He heard that his monkey’s cultivation realm was quite high. How could he cultivate without spirit stones? Breathing air?

“I didn’t save any spirit stones, not a single one... Therefore, when I don’t have any spirit stones, I can only borrow some,” Song Shuhang said.

“How much do you owe?” Papa Song said worriedly.

He was the type of person who would feel uneasy when he owed others money. After owing others money, he would be eager to return the money as soon as he had money. He would feel uneasy if he owed it for a long time.

Therefore, when he heard that Song Shuhang owed someone spirit stones, he was a little worried.

“Senior White, how many spirit stones do I owe you now?” Song Shuhang turned his head and asked.

At this time, Senior White was squatting beside the coffee table, playing with the mechanical girl on the coffee table and trying to feed her snacks.

After hearing Song Shuhang’s question, he seriously thought about it and replied, “Yes, a lot.”

“Dad, I owe you a lot, a lot,” Song Shuhang turned around and said.

Papa Song was speechless.

How much was a lot?

With his son’s salary, would he be able to repay the debt?

Chapter 2912: Ball Song Coldly Sneers

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

If Song Shuhang owed ordinary money, Papa Song would have gritted his teeth and, taking advantage of his rejuvenated body, worked for a few more years to help his son pay off his debts.

But his son owed spirit stones, and Papa Song was powerless—after all, he had no idea how to earn spirit stones.

Where could he work to earn spirit stones? He was anxious!

Senior White carefully broke open a piece of biscuit-like snack and handed a small piece to the mechanical girl, Little Ling Xiao. Then, he looked at the anxious Papa Song and comforted him, “Don’t worry. I don’t charge interest. Shuhang can pay me back slowly.”

After Senior White comforted him, Papa Song became even more worried. He didn’t even want the interest and only wanted to recover the principal? Wasn’t this just acknowledging that it was very difficult to get back the money he had borrowed and simply wanting to break even?

Song Shuhang saw that his father was still anxious, so he could only comfort him in detail. “Dad, don’t think too much about it. It’s not what you think. Senior White simply doesn’t want any interest, and it could be considered a small benefit for the younger generation. Besides, I’m going to earn spirit stones in the future. I have a big project in my hands. If I manage it well, I might even become the richest man in the cultivation world in the future. There’s still a chance to pay off the debt.”

Papa Song was speechless.

You can’t even afford half a spirit stone, and you’re talking to me about becoming the richest man in the cultivation world? Where did your confidence come from?

“Yes, the cultivation chat client is indeed a good project.” Senior White sat cross-legged on the floor and stretched out his hand to gently touch the mechanical girl. Because Little Ling Xiao hadn’t completely transformed yet, her lower body was in the shape of an eggshell. Senior White stretched out his hand and gently pushed her, making her body start to shake like a roly-poly doll. No matter how hard she shook, she wouldn’t fall down.

Little Ling Xiao swayed in circles, letting out a string of joyful laughter. Children were like this. As long as someone teased them, they would be happy.

After hearing Senior White’s words, Papa Song slightly nodded and let out a sigh of relief. It seemed that his son had really found a good project to make money.

This was the weight of words.

Because Song Shuhang was a son, Papa Song and the others had a fixed impression of him since he was young. Therefore, no matter how good Song Shuhang’s words sounded, Papa Song didn’t dare to believe them.

However, Senior White was different. As long as he casually said something, Papa Song would believe most of it. Then, with the help of Bai’s special charm, this belief would be firmly established.

At the side of the coffee table, Senior White was a little tired of playing with Ling Xiao.

After pondering for a moment, he stretched out his finger and performed the [Cleansing Dust Mantra]’s dao seal in front of Little Ling Xiao, as well as demonstrating the [Cleansing Dust Mantra]’s runes.

At the same time, he said to Song Shuhang, “Right, Shuhang. Northern River’s Loose Cultivator asked me in a private chat just now, ‘How many disciples have you taken in? How many children? He can prepare the red packet.’”

“Are reserve disciples considered disciples?” Song Shuhang asked. He suddenly thought of Joseph.

Joseph was a very persistent guy. After he decided that Song Shuhang was his wet father, he not only bought a house near Jiangnan University Town but also bought a house next door to Song Shuhang’s hometown in Wenzhou City.

Although he was still a preparatory disciple, Song Shuhang had left him a disciple position in his heart after the incident with Evil Wang.

“It can be counted... This time, you and Fellow Daoist Yellow Mountain will work together to give the members of the group treasures that can condense and strengthen the weapon spirit. The fellow daoists won’t mind if you give them more red packets,” Senior White replied.

“Then I’ll call Joseph along,” Song Shuhang said.

After saying that, he stretched out his hand and drew a line in the void, opening his Inner World.

[My son’s spatial ability?] Papa Song went up and took a glance—was trash supposed to be thrown into this space tunnel?

Eh? Something’s not right!

Inside this spatial passageway was a fairyland. Birds were singing, and flowers were fragrant. There was a clean and comfortable aura that assaulted one’s senses.

Was such a fairyland used to throw trash?

Just as he was thinking, several figures flew out of this space.

“Master, is there anything you need?” This was his eldest disciple, the monster bird Little Cai.

Little Cai had taken the treasure that Song Shuhang had brought from the Black Dragon World, which was called ‘forming a human form in advance.’ Although she hadn’t reached the Fifth Stage Realm yet, she could already transform into a human.

Usually, she preferred the state of Cai Que. This state was more suitable for her to practice dual-blade techniques.

However, today was special, so she transformed into the appearance of a multicolored girl—the same girl that she had looked like when she met the monster hunter uncle.

Then, a girl in a long black dress and black stockings stepped out of the spatial passageway. The girl was slender and tall. Other than being a little flat, there was almost no fault with her figure.

“Chu Chu greets Master.” Chu Chu bowed politely. She was a disciple of a cultivation family, so she paid more attention to etiquette.

At the same time, she bowed to Senior White, Song Shuhang’s pendant, Immortal Fairy White Bones, and the other seniors.

Although she was the second disciple, Chu Chu was more suitable to hold up the front of Song Shuhang’s faction than Little Cai.

Song Shuhang smiled and nodded at the two disciples. It would be appropriate to hand over the task of welcoming the seniors of the Nine Provinces Number One Group to Chu Chu.

‘Another two little fairies.’ Mama Song looked at Little Cai and Chu Chu with great attention. She and Papa Song were prepared to help Song Shuhang during the new year, so she had to be careful of any fairy.

Regrettably, these two fairies were Song Shuhang’s disciples, and in this day and age, teacher-student relationships were under a lot of pressure.

“Also, the tree monster Miruru, whom you borrowed from the Dream Realm to become a part of the World Tree Project, is also a disciple that I’m going to take in. She will inherit my daoist name, ‘Priest Mu.’ There’s also a preparatory disciple, Joseph. I’m thinking of giving him the Daoist name of Baijing Street’s Sabersman,” Song Shuhang said.

As he spoke, he extended his hand into his Inner World. He placed his hands on his ribs and carried out the silver-haired girl, Li Yinzhu, who had fallen asleep again.

“As for daughters, Yinzhu and Little Ling Xiao are both my daughters in a sense,” Song Shuhang said.

Senior White nodded and said, “Alright, I’ll inform Fellow Daoist Northern River.”

“How can you carry a child like this?” At this time, Mama Song came out of the room and saw Song Shuhang holding Li Yinzhu by her ribs. Therefore, she took the soft Li Yinzhu from his hands and said, “Right, should we show Apocalypse War during the new year?” A few months ago, your father wanted to play your movie in the living room during the new year so that all the relatives could see it.”

“If I play that movie, I might be beaten to death after it ends,” Song Shuhang said.

Pa ~ At this time, Little Ling Xiao, who was sitting on Senior White’s coffee table, suddenly snapped her fingers.

Then, the magic halo of the Dust Cleansing Spell condensed from her fingers and spread to every room, enveloping the entire house.

Senior White cleaned the dust in the house, while Little Ling Xiao cleaned the outside of the house.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

Papa Song couldn’t help but glance at his son.

Song Shuhang was stunned for a moment.

“As expected of my daughter! This talent in spells is deeply inherited from me,” Song Shuhang nodded.

“Kekeke ~” Little Ling Xiao let out a string of chicken-like laughter.

On the other side, in the main world, the solar system.

Ball Song hid alone in the void of the solar system, carefully observing the state of the sun.

As it lurked, it glanced at the blue Earth.

“It’s going to be the new year... This year, I want to celebrate the new year with my main body.” Ball Song made up his mind.

Then, it locked onto the position of the sun.

After investigating the Stellar Destruction Virus for so long, it finally caught the tail of the person who spread the virus behind the scenes!

This person was preparing to release the virus into the sun.

“How can I let you ruin my chance to celebrate the new year with my main body?” Ball Song said mercilessly.

Chapter 2913: Experienced Ball

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

“It’s the perfect time to capture this guy. On New Year’s Day, I’ll pack him up and present him to the main body as a New Year’s gift,” Ball Song thought to himself.

Recently, the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’ had been giving the main body a headache. So, if he could catch the mastermind behind the spread of the Stellar Destruction Virus, it would be a significant achievement.

Moreover, this would give him an excuse to return and reunite with the main body.

Thinking of this, Ball Song wished he could immediately take action and capture the person behind the virus’s spread, then bring him to see the main body.

Every time he parted ways with the main body, his inner impulse to “find the main body” would begin to accumulate. This impulse would grow stronger over time.

Each time he located the main body’s position and found him, this accumulated impulse would transform into a sense of accomplishment. It was like finding an opponent in a game of hide-and-seek, making Ball Song happy.

“However, I need to be careful now,” Ball Song said calmly.

He wanted to wait for the mastermind to officially enter the sun before activating the ‘space lockdown’ method he had secretly set up nearby, making it impossible for the mastermind to escape even if he had wings. Then, he would capture him in one move!

He wanted to capture him alive and bring him back. Of course, if he couldn’t control him, he couldn’t do anything about it. In any case, he believed that with the main body’s extraordinary methods, even if he brought back a corpse, the main body would be able to extract a lot of key information.

“Calm down, calm down. Just a little more,” Ball Song thought to himself.

At the same time, the urge to find the main body was accumulating within him.

However, he had to endure it now.

The greater the desire to find the main body was suppressed, the stronger the sense of accomplishment would be when he found him.

Ball Song had completely concealed his aura, so no one could detect him.

At the same time, at a very suitable moment, Ball Song secretly disturbed the heavenly secrets near the sun’s star, making it impossible for people to use ‘divination techniques,’ ‘crisis intuition,’ and ‘omen sense’ to predict the development of events in this area!

The experts of the present world had a strong sense of danger. If the heavenly secrets weren’t disturbed, the mastermind might sense it and become vigilant.

Ball Song was very experienced in this area.

This was an instinct engraved in his bones!

Although he had no detailed memories, he felt that he had often fought with a powerful existence in the past. Both sides had won and lost.

This memory had become Ball Song’s instinct. It allowed him to calculate the enemy in secret with ease and experience.

In particular, his method of disturbing the heavenly secrets was very gentle, as if he were stirring water... Ball Song was confident that even if the main body’s incarnation of the ruler of the Netherworld weren’t paying attention, he wouldn’t notice that the heavenly secrets had been disturbed!

In the modern world, Wenzhou City.

After summoning his disciples and daughter, Song Shuhang sighed with emotion, and said, “Unfortunately, time is a little tight. Otherwise, I could have gone to the Black Dragon World and set up the trial passageway... There’s also a preparatory disciple, Chi Tong.”

Chi Tong was a bit special. As long as his realm hadn’t reached the target, Song Shuhang wouldn’t take him out of the Black Dragon World.

“Cleansing Mantra!” Just as Song Shuhang was sighing with emotion, another cloth-purifying magical technique was thrown at him.

Song Shuhang turned his head and saw Little Ling Xiao giggling at him.

The little fellow’s talent in magic was amazing.

Senior White seemed to be interested. He sat on the floor beside the coffee table and began to teach Little Ling Xiao basic magical techniques one after another. Teaching Little Ling Xiao was much more convenient than teaching Song Shuhang. At the very least, he didn’t have to simplify magical techniques into runes.

Moreover, Little Ling Xiao learned very quickly.

From the Dust Cleansing Curse to the current Clothes Cleansing Curse, Senior White began to teach basic lightning techniques, and Thrice Reckless invented the Charging Technique.

Senior White only needed to briefly explain the principle, demonstrate it once, and then analyze the dao seal and the tricks of circulating spiritual energy. Little Ling Xiao would be able to grasp the spell after silently calculating a few chapters.

For example, now...

“Pa, zi, zi ~” The little fellow stretched out her hand and drew a line of lightning on her fingertip.

Then, she reached out and tapped on Papa Song’s phone, charging it up.

If this went on, before Song Shuhang could become the Master of All Spells, the little fellow might be able to sit on the throne of the Master of All Spells.

“Aww, my little cutie, you’re really amazing,” Papa Song praised happily. This was the privilege of a granddaughter. No matter what her granddaughter did, even if it was just climbing a few steps, she would be praised by the whole family, not to mention a practical spell like the battery charging technique.

“Congratulations, Shuhang. Although you’re still a long way from becoming the Master of All Spells, you’re one step closer to becoming the Master of All Spells’ father,” Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said happily.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

He stretched out his hand and pressed it on Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword’s body, and with a swipe of his right hand, he released 100 flashes of the Shut Up·Saber Nurturing Technique.

“Then let’s learn some more difficult spells. Hmm, let’s learn the Heavenly Master’s Lightning Technique: Five-Blow-Thunderstruck. Shuhang, open up your Inner World. Five-Blow-Thunderstruck is a little too loud, and it’s not easy to demonstrate it in the main world. Let’s go to your Inner World to practice,” Senior White said.

Five-Blow-Thunderstruck was a lightning technique that Big Boss Tyrannical Song had relied on his realm to strengthen to the level of ‘Five Thunders’. It was a lightning technique that was very memorable.

“Alright ~” Song Shuhang said.

It was finally his chance to show off.

The huge Inner World was one of the few projects that Song Shuhang could take out.

“Where should I set up the Inner World?” Senior White asked.

Song Shuhang pointed at his own room and said, “Let’s set it at the entrance of my room.”

After saying this, Song Shuhang stretched out his hand and opened the exit of the Inner World once again. This time, he set up a stable temporary passage, and the entrance overlapped with his own.

Papa Song curiously leaned over and took a look.

“Eh? Isn’t this the junkyard you mentioned before?” Papa Song said.

Song Shuhangwas confused.

Papa Song quickly realized that he had misunderstood.

As he spoke, he moved closer and looked into the Inner World curiously.

Coincidentally, when Papa Song leaned over, he saw a tall woman holding a kitchen knife and appearing aggressively.

Papa Song subconsciously stepped aside.

“Tyrannical Song, are the ingredients ready?” Immortal Fairy Bie Xue called out.

For Sage White’s sake, she was willing to help the Nine Provinces Number One Group prepare the New Year’s feast. However, Tyrannical Song hadn’t provided her with enough ingredients for the annual banquet.

“What ingredients do you want?” Song Shuhang asked.

Immortal Fairy Bie Xue pondered for a moment and said, “How about a dragon beast feast? Slaughter a dragon beast during the New Year?”

“Dragon beast? Kill the dragon? Isn’t that too cruel?” Song Shuhang asked.

Just as he said ‘kill the dragon’... Suddenly, a spatial rift opened up in the void, and a white dragon head emerged from it.

The White Dragon was speechless.

Chapter 2914: I Have a Wish

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Song Shuhang was speechless.

“Big Sister White Dragon, does your timing really have to be so coincidental?”

For a moment, he wondered if White Dragon had been peeping at him all along, just waiting for the right moment to appear.

The situation was extremely awkward.

Song Shuhang looked at White Dragon, and White Dragon stared back at him.

Immortal Fairy Bie Xue didn’t dare to say anything.

“Hey, Big Sister White Dragon, is your seclusion over?” Song Shuhang revealed a textbook smile to break the silence.

White Dragon rolled her eyes and turned into a pure white dragon. “I’m a White Dragon that’s as dead as can be. I don’t need to do things like seclusion. Sixteen is the one in seclusion on the mysterious island, not me.”

“Then has Sixteen finished her seclusion?” Song Shuhang took the opportunity to ask the key question. Previously, he had used the ‘cultivation chat’ function to privately chat with White Dragon, but White Dragon didn’t answer him.

“Probably.”

Song Shuhang was startled.

An uncertain answer?

“Right, Shuhang, do you want to become a dragon?” White Dragon suddenly asked.

“Huh?”

“Dragon!” Little Ling Xiao waved his arms excitedly. “Become a dragon!”

She had the ability to transform. In the future, as long as she had a better grasp of her own body, she could change her mechanical mode at will. Turning into a mechanical dragon would not be a problem.

“As a descendant of the dragon, are you interested in becoming a dragon?” White Dragon asked again.

“I might have been interested when I was young,” Song Shuhang replied seriously. “But now, I’ve grown up.”

I’m already a mature Tyrannical Song.

Papa Song was speechless.

Because, for a moment, he had a strong interest in becoming a dragon. To be honest, Papa Song wanted to become a dragon.

However, his son’s answer cut off his thoughts. He had already grown up, so why would he be interested in becoming a dragon? If he said that he was interested in becoming a dragon, did that mean he was not as mature as his son?

“I feel that you should consider turning into a dragon. I have a perfect method for humans to turn into dragons... well, at least the theory is very mature. You’re now a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender. If you don’t want to remain human and become a dragon, it’ll be easier for you to do so.” White Dragon’s body emerged from space and wrapped around Song Shuhang’s neck like a scarf.

Because White Dragon’s aura was too strong, Zither Master Feng Yi’s claws on her shoulder were pushed to the side, and she didn’t dare to say anything.

“After becoming a dragon, you can cut yourself as you wish. Dragon liver, dragon heart, dragon skeleton... You can cut them out and turn them into ingredients for the New Year’s banquet. Isn’t it great?” White Dragon tightened her scarf and whispered in Song Shuhang’s ear in a charming voice, “Also, dragon liver can be sold for spirit stones. It’s very popular in the cultivation world.”

After hearing White Dragon’s devilish enticement, Song Shuhang was almost tempted.

He had Cheng Lin’s Self-Healing Technique, the Primary Instruction of the Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique, and all kinds of powerful self-healing methods, just like how he had taken out 66 hearts to refine weapons previously. As long as he was willing, he could even fork out a few hundred dragon livers. If there was a buyer willing to pay spirit stones, he could even spend his entire life until the buyer went bankrupt!

“However, I refuse this method of earning money.” Song Shuhang’s heart was firm, and he wasn’t tempted at all. “No matter what falls from my body, the Giant Turtle of Disaster will come and collect it.”

“You’re not Fairy Skylark,” White Dragon said.

“It was different in the past,” Song Shuhang said. “But it’s almost the same now.”

White Dragon was speechless.

In other words, it hasn’t been long since Sixteen and I left you, and you’ve become even more troublesome?

Your ability to continuously add +1 points to your hand is really enviable.

After a long while, White Dragon sighed.

“Hahaha.” Song Shuhang didn’t know how to respond, so he could only smile politely.

“If you could advance like a normal cultivator...” White Dragon looked up at the sky. “Forget it. It’s already impossible.”

Song Shuhang was speechless.

“Are you guys busy now?” White Dragon asked as she glanced at Senior White.

Senior White nodded. “I’m a little busy. I have to make arrangements for the New Year. Shuhang will also have to stay behind to help.”

“Can you lend us his head for a while? It’ll only take a while,” White Dragon asked.

Senior White replied, “Sure.”

After getting Senior White’s approval, White Dragon tightened the scarf again.

“Stop, stop! Sister White Dragon, I’m going to die! I’m going to die!” Song Shuhang patted White Dragon and called out.

White Dragon said, “Shuhang... lend me your good head.”

Song Shuhang:

“The body will stay behind to assist Fellow Daoist White. The head will follow me first,” White Dragon said.

Song Shuhang said, “Wait a moment. You’ll scare my dad and the others. Why don’t I ask Fellow Daoist Evil Corpse to go with you?”

“No need, just follow the head,” White Dragon said.

Song Shuhang had no choice but to call out to Papa Song. “Dad, I have to leave my head for a while. Don’t worry about me.”

Papa Song was confused.

Then, under Papa Song’s horrified gaze, Song Shuhang’s head and body separated, and White Dragon carried him into the void and disappeared.

Papa Song was speechless.

F*ck, my son’s head flew away just like that?

“Won’t he die?” Papa Song looked at the severed head. No blood spurted out.

“Don’t worry, Uncle Song,” Soft Feather comforted him. “Senior Song’s flying head technique is really good.”

“Can cultivators do this?” Papa Song still felt that the scene was terrifying.

“Not everyone can do it. It’s even rarer to see someone like Senior Song who can ‘act separately,’” Soft Feather said.

“Shuhang’s body, let’s continue setting up the Inner World. Yinzhu, Chu Chu, and Little Cai, come over and follow me,” Senior White said happily.

He was prepared to let Yinzhu and the others watch from the side while he was teaching Little Ling Xiao some magical techniques. They wanted to see how talented Song Shuhang’s disciples were.

Song Shuhang’s body stretched out his hand and made an ‘OK’ gesture, bringing everyone into the Inner World.

Papa Song was at the back of the group.

As he walked, Papa Song subconsciously reached into his pocket. Looking at his headless son, he wanted to chew a few pills to calm himself down.

No matter what kind of pill it was, he just wanted to chew two.

On the other side, the mysterious island, the White Dragon Tomb.

White Dragon brought Song Shuhang’s head back to the tomb.

Next to the dragon tomb, Su Clan’s Sixteen was still meditating with her eyes closed.

However, when White Dragon returned, Su Clan’s Sixteen, who was cultivating, opened her eyes as if she had sensed Song Shuhang’s aura.

She looked at the head that was Song Shuhang and was slightly stunned.

“There’s only one head left?”

Then, she stretched out her arm.

White Dragon gently tossed Song Shuhang’s head to Sixteen.

“You’re awake, Sixteen,” Song Shuhang greeted with a smile.

“Her seclusion has ended,” Su Clan’s Sixteen corrected him as she hugged Song Shuhang’s head.

“Hahahaha.” Song Shuhang laughed awkwardly. After all, he was the only one who needed to ‘wake up’ to end his closed-door training. “Did your training go well?”

“It has been progressing step by step,” Su Clan’s Sixteen said. “However, Shuhang, you’re already a Tribulation Transcender with three corpses. It’s too fast.”

It was so fast that she didn’t have time to do many things, and Song Shuhang had already finished.

“Shuhang, I have a wish,” Su Clan’s Sixteen said.

Su Clan’s Sixteen once had a wish... before entering the final trial of the Spirit River Su Clan, she had a wish.

Chapter 2915: Therefore, We Can’t Wait Any Longer

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Su Clan’s Sixteen lifted Song Shuhang’s head with both hands and said, “Shuhang, do you want to guess what Sixteen’s wish was?”

“Wish?” Song Shuhang looked at her and pondered.

The White Dragon was swimming around randomly in the void. No matter how sweet their conversation was, the scene in front of me was still extremely terrifying.

Even though she was the one who brought Song Shuhang’s head back, she couldn’t help but complain.

“Have you guessed it?” Su Clan’s Sixteen asked.

“Marry me?” Song Shuhang said somewhat shyly.

It wasn’t that he was narcissistic. This was the answer Su Clan’s Sixteen had personally hinted to him.

At that time, Song Shuhang hadn’t reached the Profound Sage Realm and was still a newbie. Then, one day, Su Clan’s Sixteen’s aura suddenly exploded, and she insisted on discussing with him about ‘future, Dao-companion,’ and other profound questions.

At that time, Song Shuhang’s mentality wasn’t as mature as it was now, and his experience wasn’t as rich as it was now.

Song Shuhang still remembered that Sixteen had asked him if he would consider the option of getting married in the future. The main reason was that Su Clan’s Sixteen was too domineering at that moment, and he would never forget it.

He suspected that if Su Clan’s Sixteen had been a little stronger back then, he might have cowered and agreed to marry into the Spirit River Su Clan.

“Pfft,” the White Dragon couldn’t help but laugh when she heard this answer. No matter what, Tyrannical Song is an existence that can stop babies from crying in the universe. Your answer... Was he possessed?

Pavilion Master Chu, who was standing on top of Song Shuhang’s head, was speechless. Pavilion Master Chu felt a little embarrassed, and she was considering whether she should retract her hair back into her Inner World.

“Why do you still remember this?” Su Clan’s Sixteen said somewhat unnaturally. However, she didn’t wait for Song Shuhang’s reply. She continued, “Before Sixteen entered the final trial of the Spirit River Su Clan, she had a wish. She wanted to live to see you again.”

It was a wish that was both simple and very complicated. At that time, Su Clan’s Sixteen’s heavenly tribulation had not only injured her body but also her soul, which was very troublesome.

“Now, Sixteen’s wish has been fulfilled.” Su Clan’s Sixteen said as she raised Song Shuhang’s head high. At the same time, the ‘glass heart’ in her chest stepped on the accelerator and began to beat faster.

She seemed a little nervous. Pavilion Master Chu was dumbfounded. “That’s the upgraded version of Sixteen’s original wish,” Su Clan’s Sixteen said.

Song Shuhang was silent for a moment. At this time, he noticed that Su Clan’s Sixteen had been calling herself ‘Sixteen’ while introducing her ‘wish.’ Although it was a little cute, Song Shuhang felt that something was wrong when she repeatedly called herself ‘Sixteen’ at this time.

He looked at the White Dragon from the corner of his eye. Then, he noticed that the White Dragon seemed to be frowning as well, thinking about something.

The dragon tomb quieted down, leaving only the sound of Liu Li’s heartbeat.

Su Clan’s Sixteen seemed to be nervous. Song Shuhang was also very nervous. Several guesses appeared in his mind. More than half of these guesses were worrying.

Azurite’s heartbeat was still steadily accelerating. After feeling that the ‘glass heart’ was about to reach its limit, Song Shuhang finally prepared himself to withstand the impact.

Then, he braced himself and asked, “Sixteen Two?”

This was the reason why Song Shuhang was so nervous. During the process of Su Clan’s Sixteen’s final trial by fire of the Spirit River Su Clan, more than a hundred different ‘Little Sixteen’ were collected. Was Su Clan’s Sixteen still the same person from the beginning? Could it be that he had already quietly become Su Clan’s Sixteen Two?

Song Shuhang had similar concerns in the past. At that time, he had secretly used the ‘secret appraisal technique’ on Sixteen and asked the White Dragon for confirmation. Back then, the answer pointed to ‘Sixteen is still Sixteen.’ Even though she had transformed into a dragon, her essence had never changed.

But now, Song Shuhang could no longer be sure of the answer he had given earlier. This was because Su Clan’s Sixteen’s every word and action was strange. If he thought about it carefully...Actually, from the moment Sixteen came out of seclusion, some changes had occurred.

At the time, Song Shuhang thought that Sixteen’s personality had changed after experiencing the ups and downs of life and death. But now, thinking about it carefully, it was extremely terrifying.

Song Shuhang looked at Su Clan’s Sixteen’s lips, waiting for her to answer. He had already prepared himself for the worst. However, if the person in front of him was Sixteen Two, would he be able to face her calmly?

Even the White Dragon was staring at Sixteen. It seemed that even she did not notice the abnormality in this aspect? Or perhaps, when the White Dragon was possessing Sixteen’s body, she had been in contact with Sixteen Two?

Below, Su Clan’s Sixteen shook her head. Song Shuhang heaved a sigh of relief.

Just now, there was mist rising from Song Shuhang’s head, and the smell of a ghost film was very strong... However, an expert at the White Dragon’s level could tell with a glance that the fog was caused by the aura of Song Shuhang’s path to immortality.

Not only did he advance quickly, but he also had to condense the path to immortality in such a hurry?

What a good curve to overtake.

He had also experienced the Golden Core stage before. At that time, he drew seven Golden Core compositions in one go, almost driving him crazy.

The Golden Core composition, especially the finishing touch, was like a soybean milk machine.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

A hundred Little Sixteens could actually help him draw the Golden Core composition!

Back then, when I was in the Sixth Stage, if there were a hundred little Shuhangs in my body...

Song Shuhang imagined this scene. If there were a hundred little Shuhangs in the space of his consciousness...

Well...

Forget it.

Mother Yellow Mountain was already very tired, so he didn’t want to add to his burden!

Song Shuhang almost thought that Senior Yellow Mountain was monitoring him.

Perhaps Venerable Yellow Mountain had set up some sensitive words, and as long as he thought of the words ‘Mother Yellow Mountain,’ Senior Yellow Mountain would be able to sense it?

Song Shuhang said, “Here you go, dear customer!”

Senior White had teamed up with Soft Feather to hunt down the “Year Beast” for the New Year feast, and now there were only about fifty minutes left until the New Year.

On the other end, Senior White answered the call and said, “Shuhang, Soft Feather and I are taking a quick detour, but we’ll be back soon. Just tell Fairy Snow to wait ten minutes.”

“A detour? Did you find something interesting, Senior White?” Song Shuhang asked curiously.

Senior White never missed an opportunity to find treasures, and if he was taking a detour, it had to be either a valuable find or something particularly fun that had caught his attention.

“Since the New Year is almost here, even if I found something fun, I’d bring you all along. This time, it’s serious business,” Senior White replied with a smile. “I suddenly remembered the ‘Jade Pool Heavenly Court fragment’ we took from the ‘Limitless Demon Sect.’ I’m heading there now to bring it back.”

“Oh, right, the Jade Pool! I almost forgot about it too,” Song Shuhang said.

The Heavenly Court fragment of the Jade Pool, along with the Divine Lantern of Mount Lu Demon Sovereign, had been snatched from the Limitless Demon Sect.

Now, the Mount Lu Demon Sovereign was in Song Shuhang’s “Domination Realm,” overseeing the enslaved disciples of the Limitless Demon Sect—who were bound by a contract to work for Song Shuhang for free for ten years.

Originally, these disciples were to work in Song Shuhang’s Core World, but he had temporarily transferred them to the Domination Realm for the New Year feast preparations.

After all, it was all Song Shuhang’s territory. Once their ten-year contract ended, he could consider moving the entire Limitless Demon Sect into the Domination Realm as the sole resident sect. By then, they could work for Song Shuhang for compensation instead of for free.

In fact, the disciples of the Limitless Demon Sect in the Domination Realm were already so awed by Domination Song’s methods that they were left speechless.

Not only did he possess an incomparably vast personal world, but Domination Song also had an entire “multiverse!”

How... How did our young master, Sea King, manage to offend such a being?

The Sea King has led us astray!

But... maybe this is a blessing in disguise?

Domination Song’s “multiverse” world seemed to lack people. Perhaps this was an opportunity for the Limitless Demon Sect?

After finishing his conversation with Senior White, Song Shuhang turned to Chu Chu and said, “Chu Chu, go tell Fairy Snow that Senior White and the others will be back in at most ten minutes. The seniors in the group should be arriving soon... You go help Fairy Snow with the preparations. Xiao Cai, you help too.”

Xiao Cai wasn’t much help with cooking, but her knife skills could come in handy.

“Alright, Teacher,” Chu Chu nodded.

She was now pursuing the path of the Immortal Chef, so assisting Fairy Snow White was a form of cultivation for her.

“By the way, has Joseph shown up yet?” Song Shuhang asked, puzzled.

He had messaged Joseph a few days ago, intending to formally establish their master-disciple relationship during this New Year celebration.

Given Joseph’s personality, he should have already arrived by now.

But with the New Year fast approaching, Joseph was still nowhere to be seen.

“Maybe give him a call?” The Ghost Fairy, controlling Su Clan’s Sixteen’s body, hovered behind Song Shuhang, wrapping her arms around his neck.

“I’ll try,” Song Shuhang said as he pulled out his phone and selected Joseph’s name.

But as soon as the phone rang twice, the line went dead.

Song Shuhang was confused.

Joseph would never deliberately turn off his phone... Could it have been stolen?

With a slight shift of his mind, Song Shuhang channeled a bit of his primordial spirit, and in the next instant, his “Tribulation Immortal-level” divine sense enveloped the entirety of China.

His divine sense spread out silently, unnoticed by cultivators below his level.

In a mere moment, Song Shuhang pinpointed Joseph’s location.

Sure enough, Joseph was in trouble. At that moment, he was bound tightly and hanging from the ceiling of a cave, spinning slowly.

Opposite him, a crude puppet was crushing a cellphone.

“Your master’s call, but don’t think he can save you,” the crude puppet sneered. “No matter who your master is, they can’t save you.”

“Yeah! I can ask my master for help!” Joseph suddenly exclaimed.

The crude puppet was confused.

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Since Joseph had been captured, the thought of asking his master for help hadn’t crossed his mind.

For one, he was too nervous. And two, this was his first time experiencing something straight out of a martial arts novel—being captured by the villain and interrogated for treasure. In the midst of the adrenaline rush, he lacked the experience to know what to do.

After being captured, he briefly considered calling the police. But his phone, smartwatch, and any other communication devices were quickly confiscated by his captors. Clearly, these people weren’t the kind of isolated martial artists from novels, completely ignorant of modern technology.

Actually, if Joseph had mentioned his master, “Song Shuhang,” earlier, or if he had called out for his master, Song Shuhang would have sensed it immediately and located him. Given Song Shuhang’s current level, he could definitely do that. After all, Song Shuhang was now a “Tri-Sage Immortal,” and his spiritual senses were more than sharp enough to detect such things.

Unfortunately, Joseph was too tense to think of that before.

It wasn’t until the rough-looking puppet before him let out a sneering laugh that he suddenly remembered—maybe he could just shout for his master, Song Shuhang!

His master, Song Shuhang, was far more powerful than any “martial arts master” in those novels. Thinking back to the “evil obsession incident,” Joseph realized that his master was more like one of the celestial beings from Chinese legends than a mere martial artist.

Though he wasn’t sure why such a celestial being would still be a student at Southeast University, perhaps his master was one of those legendary beings who enjoyed wandering the mortal world?

So maybe, if he shouted for his master, it would work! If his master was indeed a celestial being, he might be able to hear him!

“You’re still thinking of asking for help? Do you have some hidden spell for that?” The rough puppet immediately pressed its hand to the ground, activating several array patterns that rose up in a barrier, blocking any magical rescue signals.

Better safe than sorry!

Even though this Western man had lousy skills and was no longer young, his master was probably some half-baked Western holy light cultivator.

But the rough puppet was cautious by nature, so it still raised a barrier, cutting off any unexpected rescues.

Within this barrier, no matter what kind of help Joseph tried to call for, there was no way for any signal to get out!

As the barrier activated, the rough puppet bared its sharp steel teeth, staring at Joseph—go ahead, try your rescue spell!

When you realize your spell can’t break through the barrier, that’s when you’ll lose all hope!

Under the puppet’s cold gaze, Joseph opened his mouth and yelled, “Master! Help! Help me! Save me!”

There was no hidden rescue spell, no “signal-breaking rune,” or anything like that.

Joseph’s idea of calling for help was just to shout.

The rough puppet was speechless.

I can’t believe I actually fell for this foreigner’s nonsense, actually believing this low-level guy might have some high-level rescue spell or rune to save his life!

But after all that, he’s just yelling at the top of his lungs.

It felt like my intelligence had been dragged down to his level, only to be rubbed in the dirt by his abundant experience in stupidity.

At that moment, the rough puppet felt an overwhelming urge to bash this Western middle-aged man to pieces.

“Shut up!” the rough puppet shouted in anger. “Do you really think shouting is going to get anyone to hear you? Your master can’t hear your screams; he’s not coming to save you! Damn it... because of your ridiculous shouting rescue plan, I wasted a barrier setup. I can’t believe I was dumb enough to think you actually had a magical rescue method. If you keep yelling, I’ll stab you in the kidney.”

Joseph remained silent.

Barrier? Magical methods?

It sounded like this creature wasn’t just an ordinary martial arts master either, but more like his master—a celestial being, perhaps even a monster from legends.

So, does that mean my master still has a chance to save me?

Joseph felt a twinge of anxiety.

“Stop thinking about your master. Whoever he is, he can’t save you now. Tell me, where did you hide my key stone disk?” the rough puppet snarled through clenched teeth.

Joseph hesitated.

*Why don’t you ask him? Why doesn’t he ask you who your master is?* Suddenly, a soft yet familiar voice echoed in Joseph’s ear.

Though the voice was youthful, it carried the weight of years and had the tone of a wise elder.

Joseph’s eyes lit up.

It was his master!

Last time, when facing the “monster in the fog,” his master’s voice had also appeared like this!

His master had heard his cries for help!

Suddenly, Joseph felt a surge of confidence.

“Hmph!” Joseph cast a haughty look down at the rough puppet—though he was still spinning while suspended from the ceiling.

“Since you’re so sure my master can’t save me, why don’t you ask who my master is?” Joseph raised his head proudly, though the action made it hard for him to breathe. But right now, he needed to exude an air of confidence!

The rough puppet said nothing.

It didn’t want to play into Joseph’s game. After all, it had already been dragged into his foolish rhythm once, getting its intelligence rubbed in the dirt.

But even if the rough puppet didn’t want to respond, Joseph wasn’t going to stop.

“My master’s name is Song Shuhang! He’s from the Jiangnan University’s Mechanical Engineering Department!” Joseph loudly proclaimed his master’s name.

Since his master had prompted him to say it, Joseph figured the puppet must recognize the name.

In Joseph’s mind, his master was akin to a legendary martial artist. Just by mentioning his name, the entire martial arts world would give him respect.

“Song Shuhang?” The rough puppet’s reaction was far more intense than Joseph had imagined!

The puppet’s entire body trembled, and it even took a few involuntary steps backward.

Judging by the way it shook in fear, it was clear that his master wasn’t just a “famous martial artist.” No, it was more like his master was the leader of the martial arts world, whose name alone struck terror in those who heard it.

“Ba... Ba Song.” The rough puppet’s voice quivered.

Once, it thought the title “Millennium’s First Sage” was a joke.

Once, it believed that Ba Song was just a little newbie at the fourth realm.

Once, it had even stabbed Ba Song in the kidney and planned to do it again.

Once, it had cursed Ba Song.

Once, it had teamed up with the Beast Cultivation Realm’s Gorilla General to deal with Ba Song.

Once, it had even worked with the Sea King to plot against Ba Song.

But all of that was in the past.

It never imagined that the Ba Song it thought was a joke would now be dominating all the immortals across the realms, and even be a top candidate for the next Heavenly Dao.

The rough puppet trembled for a full thirty seconds.

Then, it steeled itself and transformed its right hand into a sharp blade. “How could someone with your pathetic skills be his disciple? Besides... even if you are, with this barrier, he might not be able to sense this place.”

The rough puppet’s killing intent surged as it slowly stepped toward Joseph.

Suspended in the air, Joseph shivered as a cold fear spread through his body.

Each step the rough puppet took felt like it was stomping on Joseph’s heart, causing it to race faster and faster.

One step, two steps...

As the puppet took its third step, a finger materialized out of thin air, gently tapping the rough puppet’s forehead.

That single tap didn’t just target the rough puppet but traced it back to its source.

“Ba... Ba Song...” the rough puppet stammered, its voice catching as if a mechanical glitch had taken over.

These puppet avatars and their source had a very special relationship. Even if a single puppet were completely annihilated, it wouldn’t harm the source. Tracing the source through just one puppet was nearly impossible.

When Tyrannical Song’s finger touched the puppet’s forehead, it instantly bypassed hundreds of fake decoy points and broke through dozens of virtual sources to lock onto the real one!

The source of the crude puppet didn’t even have time to react... The events that unfolded were too fast for its consciousness to keep up.

The power gap between it and Dominating Song was of a different dimension entirely.

Divine techniques!

This was the standard entrance of a big shot!

Below.

The next moment, his finger pressed deeper into the crude puppet’s forehead, piercing it and leaving a hole.

Boom!

The crude puppet’s skull emitted a sound of explosion, and the puppet collapsed.

At the same time, across the heavens and realms, in nearly a hundred different world planes, close to a thousand puppets suddenly collapsed, with their skulls exploding.

Among them, some puppets were even unknown to others as puppets!

They had lived their own lives, with identities within small sects of the cultivation world.

They were like Mr. Shelan, who broke into the Chu family’s home with sea urchin warriors, trying to steal the “sword manual.” They thought they were still alive, believing only parts of their bodies had been modified and turned into puppets.

They had their own schemes, their own ambitions... their own goals and desires.

But in reality, they had long become nothing more than puppets in the hands of the “puppet source.”

These thousands of puppets were all destroyed, their heads blown to bits.

Simultaneously, the hidden “puppet source” in the shadows also disintegrated in despair.

Beside it, in a hidden cave, were countless puppet parts, cultivation techniques, pills, and treasures... but no spirit stones.

Recently, this puppet source had been keeping a low profile, afraid of being caught by Dominating Song, so its stash of spirit stones, accumulated over years, had been drained.

The liquid metal Song Shuhang gathered all these items.

After eliminating the puppet source, Ball Shuhang felt an overwhelming sense of satisfaction—playing hide and seek with the main body and then taking down an enemy afterward doubled the sense of achievement!

Chapter 2930: Ball Shuhang’s New Year’s Gift

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Indeed, after Joseph shouted “Help!” loudly, Ball Shuhang seized the opportunity and made a flashy entrance before the original body could!

Ball Shuhang had been pondering whether there was a more ingenious way to make an entrance, something that would catch the original body off guard.

For two days, it had been lingering in the solar system, using a combination of “divination methods + instinct” to track the original body’s location.

When Joseph cried out for help, Ball Shuhang knew its moment had arrived!

Without hesitation, it acted, interrupting the original body’s chance to show off—taking the path of the original body and leaving it with no way forward; stealing the spotlight so the original body couldn’t shine.

The feeling was simply indescribable.

Ball Shuhang’s instincts told it that after finally finding some satisfaction at the expense of the original body, slaying a few more things would amplify that satisfaction exponentially.

This crude puppet’s core just happened to fall into Ball Shuhang’s hands, becoming the perfect score to boost its joy.

After dealing with the core of this “crude puppet,” Ball Shuhang didn’t forget to collect the spoils of war, using spatial means to snatch everything the puppet was holding.

After all, the original body had so many workers in its core world now that anything thrown in could be transformed into something useful.

As a competent clone, Ball Shuhang was always looking out for the original body, meticulously planning.

And with the New Year countdown already underway, if it didn’t make its appearance now, it wouldn’t have time to give the original body a New Year’s gift.

Having completed everything, Ball Shuhang’s form bounced into a “liquid metal sphere,” hopping a few times on the ground before quietly waiting for the original body to arrive.

“Teacher, why did you turn into a ball?” Joseph asked, puzzled, staring at Ball Shuhang on the ground.

But he certainly couldn’t do it as cleanly as Ball Shuhang had, erasing all traces and preventing any chance of resurrection.

However, despite how perfectly everything had been set up for him to make an entrance, Ball Shuhang had swooped in and stolen the moment. Song Shuhang’s feelings were now incredibly complicated.

Ball Shuhang glanced at the original body and, upon seeing the constipated look on its face, felt a vague sense of “happiness” welling up inside.

Doing this made it happy... The satisfaction was second only to the moment it had reunited with the original body after traversing countless mountains and rivers.

This additional joy was something Ball Shuhang found addicting.

Xiao Lingxiao was also staring at Ball Shuhang.

The two shared countless connections, so even though this was their first real meeting, they felt an inexplicable resonance.

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

What do you mean *our* daughter? That’s going to cause misunderstandings!

Although Joseph practiced the “Holy Light Sword Technique,” that sword technique had been entirely modified from a “blade technique” template. With Ba Cu in his hand, Joseph could fully utilize the sword technique—Song Shuhang had experienced this firsthand.
