On the other side,

After the original body put its disciple down, Ball Shuhang reluctantly tore its gaze from “Xiao Lingxiao.”

Because of the feeling of familiarity, it really wanted to hug Xiao Lingxiao, to touch her, to connect with her.

Ball Shuhang forced itself to suppress the urge.

A New Year’s gift?

At that moment, Song Shuhang was deeply touched!

Ball Shuhang was truly the model of all clones!

Chapter 2931: Indeed, You Are Its True Form!

This guy was planning to release the virus into the Sun?

Memory extraction techniques usually involved overpowering a weaker opponent... and generally only worked on those at a lower level than oneself.

It was one thing whether he could afford it or not, but it was also very pleasing to the eye to keep it at home.

Moreover, he already had a throne.

The Thorn Crown + Endurance Throne combination, the Life-saving Survival Set.

It was much more practical than the “Heavenly Emperor Throne Two,” which was only good-looking.

At this time, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword smiled and said, “Actually, this might not be a throne. It might be”

“Fellow Daoist Scarlet Heaven Sword, be careful with your words. Tiandi Zi will still be resurrected,” Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet hurriedly reminded him.

“Don’t continue on this topic. Shuhang is still young, and he doesn’t want to die,” Pavilion Master Chu said, still in a daze.

Song Shuhang was confused.

“Seniors, what are you talking about? Why is it suddenly related to my death?”

As they were talking, the lotus projection of the Inner World impatiently extended over and shamelessly licked the Heavenly Emperor Throne Two.

“Stop! Wait a moment,” Song Shuhang stopped the Inner World from licking the “Heavenly Emperor’s path to immortality.”

In a while, the Island Master would transfer his portion of the ancient Heavenly City fragment over. Song Shuhang had promised to take good care of his fragment of the Heavenly City.

Therefore, before that, he had to train his Inner World to temporarily control its licking behavior.

After receiving Song Shuhang’s order, the lotus projection could only reluctantly retreat, turning back three times with every step it took.

“Core Assistant, move the neighboring Jade Lake Immortal Realm to the fragment of the ancient Heavenly City as well. It will provide assistance to the Great Northern Emperor and the others in their operation later. As for the Heavenly Emperor’s Throne Palace, keep it for now. It’s just a small fragment anyway,” Song Shuhang said. “It’s not appropriate to expose something like the Heavenly Emperor’s throne to the members of the ancient Heavenly City.”

“I already saw it,” Zither Master Fengyi said.

“I already saw it,” the virtuous lamia’s voice came from Song Shuhang’s stomach. She repeated Zither Master Fengyi’s words.

“I saw it too. If I saw it, it means Sixteen saw it. If Sixteen saw it, it means Big Sister White Dragon saw it,” Sixteen Cape said.

“I saw it, which means my Lord saw it too,” Senior Turtle appeared beside him at some point and reminded him.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

“If you all saw it, then why would I hide it?”

“Then let’s close this palace for now.” Senior White stretched out his hand and pressed on the key.

Then, the palace door slowly closed.

Senior White casually threw the key to Song Shuhang.

“Eh? Was it made of spirit stones? No wonder it was called the stone key. There’s nothing wrong with the spirit stone.” When Song Shuhang took the key, he could tell what material it was made of just by touching it.

Moreover, this was at least a spirit stone of the Ninth Stage.

After thinking for a moment, Song Shuhang instructed, “Little Assistant Core, record this key... The next time I spend money on it, be careful not to spend too much.”

“Recording complete” the Core Assistant replied.

Song Shuhang gently caressed this key made of a spirit stone of the Ninth Stage. This was probably the only spirit stone item he could preserve at the moment.

Senior White looked at the time and said, “Let’s go. We don’t have much time left. Let’s go find Fairy Bie Xue!”

“The countdown for the New Year is the fireworks event. Senior White and I are going to do the countdown~ I have to go back,” Soft Feather raised her hand and said happily.

In the past, she spent the New Year on Spirit Butterfly Island. Moreover, it wasn’t held every year. After all, the New Year was not a holiday that cultivators cared much about. Sometimes, Venerable Spirit Butterfly would miss it if he stayed in seclusion for too long.

This was the first time Soft Feather had spent the New Year with so many people in the Nine Provinces Number One Group. Therefore, she was especially happy and excited.

Inner World, Lakeview Villa Planning Area

Senior Yellow Mountain had also arranged a program.

After the countdown ended, the New Year banquet would begin, and the program would also start.

At this moment, on the lawn by the lake, several young figures were playing and running.

Abbot Profound Principle had brought Little Guoguo, Fairy Lychee had brought Loli Shi and Loli Zhu, True Monarch Tyrant Flood Dragon had brought a little princess, who was Yu Jiaojiao’s younger sister, Cave Lord Snow Wolf had brought two little wolves, and Doudou, who was clearly already at the Fifth Stage Realm, could still play with the little wolves.

Shi and Zhu’s laughter, the little wolf’s cries, Yu Jiaojiao’s little sister’s babbling, and Little Guoguo’s miserable cries all rang out.

Cave Lord Snow Wolf transformed into his true form and laid on the edge of the lawn, dozing off as he watched these devilish children.

Abbot Profound Principle sat next to Cave Lord Snow Wolf and clasped his hands together. Since he cultivated Silent Meditation and wouldn’t speak under normal circumstances, he might as well look after the children with Cave Lord Snow Wolf.

At the lakeside, Fairy Lychee, Fairy Sixth Cultivator of True Virtue, and Fairy Firefly were sitting on the shore, gently swaying their feet in the lake. They were talking about something in soft voices, and from time to time, a burst of pleasant laughter could be heard.

At the edge of the forest, Medicine Master and Riverly Purple Mist were sitting under a tree. They were holding a large newspaper in their hands, blocking everyone’s line of sight. They were trying to cover something up. It was unknown if Andeli was doing something that required the Holy Knight’s Holy Light to shine.

In the past, Senior Medicine Master would always exchange alchemy techniques with Senior Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue, Senior Yellow Mountain, Senior White, and the others. However, recently, he only talked about whether the dog food was good or not and gave up his main business.

Behind them, the originally bare tree could no longer bear it anymore. Beautiful plum blossoms bloomed, setting off Medicine Master and Riverly Purple Mist.

On the temporary stage, Senior Yellow Mountain and Sage Monarch Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue were working together to set up a huge calendar. At the last second of the New Year, they had to tear off the last page of the calendar and open a new chapter for the year.

Heaven Hiding Hook Zhou Li was also serving Senior Eternal Fire as if he were his father-in-law, handing over the couplet paper to him. After all, if he wanted to marry Fairy Yuqin, he had to build a good relationship with Senior Eternal Fire.

Dharma King Creation, Fairy Dongfang Six, and Palace Master Seven Lives Talisman were adjusting the electronic equipment, making the final preparations for the stage of the upcoming New Year’s Banquet.

True Monarch White Crane and Young Master Phoenix Slayer, who were in their fairy forms, were setting up the table. True Monarch White Crane was full of energy, but Young Master Phoenix Slayer was a little lazy. Winter had arrived, and he especially wanted to curl up next to the heater and roast his cat fur. He didn’t want to move.

Not far away, Seven was slashing at Thrice Reckless.

Thrice Reckless jumped up and down. Su Clan’s Seven’s face was ferocious, and he looked like an evil ghost that had just stepped out of hell. He had the aura of someone who wanted to chop Thrice Reckless into pieces for the new year.

Mama Song and Papa Song didn’t know the truth and thought this was a rehearsal for the New Year’s program. They sat together with the other members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group and acted as spectators. From time to time, they would cheer and applaud loudly.

Only the reliable Senior Northern River quietly spread out a bed and took out a healing pill.

“What a harmonious scene.” As soon as Song Shuhang entered, he saw Seven chopping Thrice Reckless, and his heart warmed up. Everyone was happy.

After seeing Song Shuhang, Senior White, Soft Feather, and the others, Immortal Fairy Bie Xue waved her hand and said, “Over here, Fellow Daoist White!”

Senior White and Soft Feather walked over, preparing to hand over the secret surprise for the New Year’s banquet the “year beast.”

Song Shuhang wanted to follow them, but Zhu ran over and tugged at his windbreaker.

“Senior Brother Song, Senior Brother Song!” Zhu called out.

“What’s the matter?” Song Shuhang asked as he picked her up.

“Where’s the snow? Isn’t it supposed to snow during the New Year?” Loli Zhu asked.

If there was no snow during the New Year, could it still be called the New Year?

“Snow?” Song Shuhang sighed. “It’s snowing all over the country, but I’m the only one in Wenzhou who doesn’t see any snow.”

Since he was young, he had only seen snow a few times in Wenzhou.

Fortunately, he was a cultivator now.

“Fairy Dongfang Snow, let’s make Wenzhou’s first snow of 2020!” Song Shuhang loudly called for help.

He, Tyrannical Song, had killed a Tribulation Transcender with three corpses. Yet, he had so many seniors one of them would surely be able to make it snow.

“Even though my Daoist name has the word ‘Xue’ in it, I don’t know how to make it snow. I’m not of the ice attribute,” Fairy Dongfang Snow replied. “Your name is Song Shuhang, but do you know how to write books?”

“I know how to read,” Song Shuhang replied earnestly.

“Actually, my master is an ice and snow type,” Senior Turtle reminded him.

Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up.

The Great Northern Emperor was not only an ice element cultivator but also a big shot who had stepped onto the path of immortality with the ice element.

So, he used the Cultivation Chat System to contact the Great Northern Emperor.

“I’m not available right now,” the senior from the north said. “I’m the Great Emperor Chang Sheng. Do you think I’d make it snow for you just like that? What about my dignity?”

Song Shuhang was speechless.

You’re the Great Emperor Chang Sheng, yet you’ve done things like peeping at screens. Why can’t you make it snow?

“In that case, what should I do to make Senior Beifang lose face?” Song Shuhang asked directly.

His life experience had taught him that as long as the price was right, anyone could set aside their dignity.

Especially the Almighty Merchant if the spirit stones were in place, he’d sell his face repeatedly.

“It’s not happening,” the Great Northern Emperor replied.

He was the one who valued face the most among the four great emperors of the celestial heavens.

“Yes, Senior Northside, did you happen to see the newly acquired ‘Heavenly Emperor Throne Two’ through Senior Turtle?” Song Shuhang asked, already knowing the answer.

The Great Northern Emperor was speechless.

“Anyway, since you’ve already seen it, I can lend the throne to you,” Song Shuhang smiled and said. “Let’s have Wenzhou City’s first snow of 2020!”

Chapter 2937: If You’re Unhappy, Come Bite Me!

So, just a few minutes later...

Heavy snow began to fall over Wenzhou City, the kind of snow that many young residents of Wenzhou had never seen in their lifetimes. It was the legendary kind of snow perfect for making snowballs, having snowball fights, building snowmen, and rolling around in the snow—enough to make most of Wenzhou’s residents transform into ecstatic huskies, frolicking in the snowy wonderland!

The snowfall blanketed every corner of Wenzhou City, and under the meticulous control of the Northern Emperor, it precisely settled on the lakeside lawn of Song Shuhang’s Core World. At that moment, there was a gateway connecting the Core World to the real world, allowing the Northern Emperor’s power to pass through.

The snow quickly accumulated, covering the grassy area around the lake with a thick layer. And the snowfall didn’t show any sign of letting up? it just kept coming down like money wasn’t an issue!

Under the influence of the Northern Emperor’s magic, the temperature in the area dropped dramatically, causing the lake to freeze over with a thick layer of ice.

“Snow Wolf, it’s too much, that’s enough,” called out Sixteen, Lychee Fairy, and Liu Ying, who had been playfully dipping their bare feet in the lake water.

The ice was forming so quickly that the three fairies found their feet trapped in it, unable to move—though, with their cultivation levels, they weren’t exactly bothered by the cold.

“It wasn’t me, I swear! Don’t accuse me falsely!” grumbled Snow Wolf Cave Lord, who was himself buried under a thick pile of snow.

Next to him was Master Tong Xuan, half-buried in the snow with his head, shoulders, and part of his body completely covered.

The little ones who had begged Song Shuhang for snow were now completely buried under it, with only their little heads sticking out, shivering from the cold.

They looked like they were learning to swim, slowly moving through the snow... Occasionally, they had to pop out like a whale breaching the surface, gasping for fresh air.

“It was a senior I invited who brought this snow, but he’s too proud to admit it,” Song Shuhang explained. “Even though he was tempted by my treasure to create this snow, his actions clearly show he’s holding a grudge against me.”

The snow was coming down so heavily—there was no way the Northern Emperor wasn’t doing it on purpose.

Such pride.

“Ah Song, heads up!” Suddenly, Li Yinzhu’s voice rang out— the little one who had been dozing off on Senior White’s lap earlier was now wide awake and full of energy.

Song Shuhang turned his head just in time to see a massive, two-meter-wide snowball flying straight at him.

Hold on! This isn’t playing snowball fights anymore!

With his current level as a Tribulation Transcender, Song Shuhang could easily dodge the snowball... but seeing the eager look on Li Yinzhu’s face, he could only smile and let the snowball hit him squarely in the face.

It didn’t hurt at all.

Boom!

The massive snowball smashed into Song Shuhang and shattered into pieces.

Thunk! Something hard seemed to hit Song Shuhang’s head with a dull thud.

He reached out and grabbed a small metallic figure that had been hidden inside the snowball—a mechanical girl...

The little ones had completely underestimated just how tough Tyrant Song’s skull was. The mechanical girl’s eyes were now flickering like strobe lights, and her internal circuits were close to short-circuiting.

As soon as Song Shuhang released his grip, the mechanical girl rolled into his arms, wobbling back and forth like a roly-poly toy.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

Only someone as childish as Doudou could come up with such an idea.

But provoking me was your biggest mistake this year, Doudou. Don’t start crying later!

“Chuchu!” Song Shuhang suddenly called out.

Chuchu looked up in his direction, confused. “Master?”

I’ve had seven titles in the past, and while ‘Virtuous Gentleman Saber’ was passed down to Little Cai, today I’m giving you a new title—’Seeker Scholar.’ When you decided to follow me, it was to ‘seek the Dao,’ to find an opportunity for enlightenment. This title suits you well. From today, you shall be known as Seeker Fairy. Witness this, everyone,” Song Shuhang announced solemnly.

Chuchu was caught completely off guard by her master’s sudden decision to give her a title.

But to her, it was like receiving the best New Year’s gift ever.

A Daoist title held special significance for a cultivator.

And when it was a meaningful title, it symbolized that the disciple’s fate was tied to their master’s.

“Thank you, Master, for bestowing this title upon me,” Chuchu said, bowing deeply.

As she bowed, she felt an immense wave of fortune and virtue settle upon her.

Tyrant Song, known for his boundless merit, was a figure whose virtue was unmatched across the heavens. Being his disciple, receiving a title from him meant being blessed with great fortune.

Chuchu felt a lightness in her body, and even her cultivation and Daoist heart seemed to improve!

This was the benefit of having a powerful master—being accepted as a disciple, receiving a title, and eventually graduating brought significant advantages.

“Focus on your cultivation. If you have any questions, you can use the ‘Cultivation Chat’ to ask the seniors in the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group,’” Song Shuhang said earnestly.

Then he looked at Doudou. “Doudou, look—there’s one less Chuchu now!”

Doudou was bewildered. “Huh?”

“From today onwards, she’s Seeker Fairy!” Song Shuhang declared proudly.

As of today, the world has one less Chuchu and one more Seeker Fairy.

“You’re such a child! Woof!” Doudou barked angrily.

Song Shuhang chuckled. “I’m her master. I have the right to do this. If you’re upset, come bite me!”

Repent, Doudou.

“If you’re still upset, I’ll post an announcement on the ‘Cultivation Chat’ to recruit a hundred cultivators named ‘Chuchu’ from across the realms to become my disciples. Then, one by one, I’ll give them all new titles... and just like that, the realms will have a hundred fewer Chuchus,” Song Shuhang said mischievously.

“Woof!” Doudou growled, charging at Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang laughed heartily. “Hahaha!”

*Thwack*—a tuft of hair from Pavilion Master Chu’s clone swatted his head. “How old are you? Stop acting like a kid. You’re a Tribulation Transcender—why are you arguing with children?”

“But Senior Chu, I’m just a few minutes away from turning nineteen,” Song Shuhang said.

*Thwack, thwack, thwack* Pavilion Master Chu’s tuft of hair kept smacking him.

The old year was about to end...

A new year was about to begin!

Nourishing silently.

Inside the Core World.

Some of the more observant seniors in the “Nine Provinces Number One Group” remained calm.

It wasn’t that they had become accustomed to Song Shuhang’s ‘deaths’ and were now indifferent to them; rather, they noticed that the Core World was still functioning normally.

The Core World, in some aspects, could represent Song Shuhang’s current state.

If Song Shuhang had truly perished, with both his body and soul obliterated, the Core World they were currently in would inevitably collapse. The rules of the Core World, which operated in sync with Song Shuhang, would also vanish.

But now, the Core World was running smoothly... it was even purifying the energy of the ‘blood-red raindrops’ falling from the sky, ensuring that the ‘Bà Sòng legacy energy’ could be absorbed more efficiently by everyone.

Aside from the Core World, the “Cultivator Chat System” that relied on Bà Sòng’s existence was also running steadily, unaffected by Song Shuhang’s first explosion of the New Year.

So, these careful seniors could confirm that Song Shuhang was definitely safe and sound.

Though they didn’t know why he had exploded again, they were sure that Song Shuhang had entered the normal ‘resurrection process.’ Before long, he would be bouncing around again, full of life.

“But... isn’t Song Shuhang a Tribulation-Transcending Immortal now? Why would he suddenly explode like that?” The seniors in the Nine Provinces Number One Group exchanged thoughts via the “Cultivator Chat System.”

Who in the world could secretly assassinate Song Shuhang so quietly that he didn’t even notice?

“I don’t think it was an assassination. If someone could silently kill Song Shuhang, they would’ve already dominated the heavens and the earth, achieving Dao of Heaven,” Seven Cultivation Holy Sovereign replied.

“Senior White, any ideas?” Yellow Mountain asked while chewing on a pill.

“None.” Senior White shook his head.

Then, he extended his arm, glancing at his wrist. “Shuhang is fine. Although his Primordial Spirit Projection was affected for a moment, it has already recovered. He’s now in the resurrection phase.”

Hidden within Senior White’s arm was Song Shuhang’s Primordial Spirit Projection.

A moment ago, Senior White’s own Primordial Spirit Projection had disintegrated alongside Song Shuhang’s sudden explosion.

“Senior White, the New Year’s Gala will proceed as usual. Please host the event... I’ll be back soon.” Song Shuhang’s voice suddenly came from Senior White’s arm.

Hearing Shuhang’s voice, the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group finally breathed a sigh of relief.

Though they had made educated guesses, they only fully relaxed after confirming that Song Shuhang was safe.

“Leave it to me. Fairy Snow Maiden, bring out the Year Beast.” Senior White called out.

Boom, boom, boom

As he spoke, another wave of ‘fireworks’ shot into the sky.

This time, they were actual fireworks.

Unbeknownst to everyone, someone had set off a row of fireworks and firecrackers by the lakeside and quietly ignited them.

The fireworks that shot up were dazzlingly beautiful, whether viewed from below or from the side.

“So pretty,” Soft Feather said as she gazed upward.

The fireworks continued to rise, their brilliance lingering.

After a long while...

The fireworks display ended.

The lights then focused on Fairy Snow Maiden.

She brought out a fierce beast with long antennae and sharp fangs.

The Year Beast, Xi!

No one had expected that Senior White would actually find and capture such a ferocious creature—originally, even Fairy Snow Maiden had only intended to catch a common, non-sentient Flood Dragon or something similar to serve as the Year Beast.

The Xi was a brutal beast without intelligence, driven purely by a desire to destroy everything. Because of its nature, it had long been hunted by cultivators, making it exceedingly rare in the current cultivation world.

What made it even more remarkable was that the Year Beast was delicious, with a particularly rich flavor.

Eating it would not only fill one’s stomach but also increase one’s cultivation.

Subduing demons and monsters to benefit the world, gaining power, and enjoying a tasty meal—it’s no wonder the Year Beast had nearly been hunted to extinction.

To survive, the Year Beast would need to be bred, but raising them had proven to be incredibly difficult. To date, there hadn’t been a successful large-scale breeding plan for Year Beasts...

At this moment, the Year Beast Xi had already been slain by Fairy Snow Maiden with a single stab to the throat in the instant everyone shouted ‘one’ and Song Shuhang exploded, the Fairy had struck, sending the beast into the afterlife.

“This Xi is a mutated variant,” Fairy Snow Maiden explained. “After I prepare it, anyone who consumes its flesh should sit down immediately to absorb the energy. Its blood and flesh offer a one-time ‘Blood Rebirth’ effect. This will work for cultivators at the seventh rank and below.”

A one-time ‘Blood Rebirth’ effect is nearly equivalent to a weak version of a ‘resurrection.’

After saying this, Fairy Snow Maiden pulled the blade from the beast’s throat.

A spray of pure energy in the form of blood mist gushed out...

The Year Beast Sacrifice began!

The Creation Law King started to play a tune in coordination.

Meanwhile, at the spot where Song Shuhang had exploded, the windbreaker that Song Fatball had transformed into was now draped over the shoulders of the dizzy Mechanical Maiden.

Su Clan’s Sixteen gently lifted the Mechanical Maiden.

Pavilion Master Chu’s ahoge moved over to Sixteen’s head.

Scarlet Heaven Sword, Nine Repair Phoenix Saber, Stone Tablet Fellow Daoist, and Phoenix Ruler Claw, among other attachments, also temporarily shifted to Spirit Ghost Fairy A’16.

In Song Shuhang’s absence, the Spirit Ghost Fairy essentially became Song Shuhang.

Su Clan’s Sixteen gazed off into the distance, her eyes fixed on the “Heavenly Emperor’s Palace.”

Within the depths of the palace, atop the Heavenly Emperor’s throne marked as “TWO,” a figure began to take shape.

It was none other than the recently exploded Bà Sòng.

At this moment, Song Shuhang hadn’t fully resurrected yet—he lingered between life and death, much like Schrödinger’s squirrel.

Inside his body, at the location of his Life Force Dantian, a rune on the forehead of the Immortal Whale Golden Core began to fade, leaving only an empty shell.

This was similar to Immortal Bone Revivals like Skylark’s.

However, Song Shuhang’s Immortal Whale Golden Core revival had a cooldown period. Once exhausted, it needed time for the color in the rune to replenish.

Song Shuhang silently sat on the throne.

He raised his palm, looking at the now-vanished red dot in his hand. “Heh heh heh, gotcha.”

“Senior Song, my mysterious island’s Heavenly Court fragment is coming!” The voice of the Island Master echoed in his mind.

“The ritual can now begin.” The Northern Emperor’s voice chimed in at the same time.

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

“Senior Island Master, you can move in whenever you’re ready. I’ve already granted you access,” Song Shuhang, who was currently hovering between life and death on the throne, said aloud.

“Got it. I’m on my way,” the Island Master replied.

Given the Golden Trigram Island Master’s current cultivation level, moving all the fragments of the Heavenly Court from the mysterious island wouldn’t be an issue at all.

After that, Song Shuhang responded to the Northern Emperor: “Senior Northern Emperor, I’ve consolidated all the fragments of the Heavenly Court into one area and separated that area from the rest of the core world. You can conduct the ceremony without any worries. However, due to some personal reasons, the Heavenly Emperor’s Throne Two will be transferred to you a bit later.”

“I understand. My Turtle has already informed me that you’ve exploded again and are currently resurrecting at the ‘Heavenly Emperor’s Palace,’” the Northern Emperor replied. “We also need to wait for Golden Trigram to move the ‘Heavenly Court fragments’ over before starting the ceremony. This buffer time should be enough for your physical body to revive.”

“That’s good to hear,” Song Shuhang replied. News sure travels fast—no sooner had he exploded than the Northern Emperor got wind of it.

“By the way, how did you explode this time?” the Northern Emperor asked, taking advantage of the brief lull before the ceremony out of curiosity.

Song Shuhang wasn’t the inexperienced “fake Profound Sage” he had been a few months ago. Now, as a genuine Tribulation Immortal who had severed three corpses, he was someone even the most powerful beings across the heavens and earth would respect as a “big shot.”

Even someone like the Northern Emperor, a top-tier immortal, couldn’t simply cause Song Shuhang to explode without any warning.

“If I told you I did it to spread some New Year’s cheer, would you believe me, Senior?” Song Shuhang responded.

The Northern Emperor paused for a moment before replying, “If it were someone else, I wouldn’t believe it. But coming from you... yeah, I actually would. It sounds like something you’d do. I’ll be sure to share this with the others.”

Song Shuhang:

Your confidence in me is too heavy, Senior Northern Emperor. I can’t bear it.

“See you in a bit,” the Northern Emperor concluded, not giving Song Shuhang a chance to explain further, and ended the call.

Back on the Heavenly Emperor’s Throne Two, Song Shuhang, still suspended between life and death, resembled a misty cloud curled up on the throne.

He tapped the armrest of the throne lightly with his fingers.

Of course, the reason he exploded wasn’t just because he wanted to.

Even though he had died countless times in the past year, he wasn’t like Yunyi Ziqi from the Profound Girl Sect, who enjoyed courting death. He wasn’t a fan of dying. If he could avoid it, he would much rather stay alive... after all, resurrection artifacts are expensive.

That said, there was a reason for this “New Year’s First Explosion” of Song Shuhang’s.

The catalyst for the explosion was related to that “Stellar Destruction Virus.”

The Stellar Destruction Virus was the fuse, while the “Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull” that Fat Ball had sealed and sent him at the end of last year served as the spark that ignited it.

During this period, Song Shuhang had intentionally suppressed his Spirit Ghost Fairy, the Merit Snake Beauty, the Nine-Repair Phoenix Sabre, and other “attachments” instead of snuffing out the spark and fuse. He had quietly cooperated instead.

Then... at the moment his body exploded, the “Cultivation Chat System” managed to lock onto an ID in the background.

To be honest, even Song Shuhang himself hadn’t expected this “follow-the-thread” tactic to be so successful.

So successful, it was like Senior White had taken over his body!

He had been prepared to use the “Law of Cause and Effect,” along with the help of the Confucian Sage’s Eye, Senior White Two, the Three-Eyed Senior, Dog Egg Dad, Song Youyou, and Lady Long Luo, to forcibly track down the existence behind the “Stellar Doomsday Demon Skull” and the “Virtual Sun Guardian.”

But before he could even make his move, the “Cultivation Chat System” quietly locked onto a user ID.

Yes... the terrifying entity behind the Virtual Sun Guardian and the Stellar Doomsday Demon had actually registered an account on the “Cultivation Chat System” and even downloaded a “client.”

And at the exact moment of Song Shuhang’s explosion, that terrifying entity launched a powerful attack on the “Cultivation Chat System,” trying to seize it for itself!

This was a true powerhouse!

Far more domineering and powerful than any of the big shots Song Shuhang had faced before!

Even the likes of Demon Emperor Hezhi couldn’t figure out how to deal with the “Cultivation Chat System” and had been toying with the idea of deleting Song Shuhang as a friend for days without success.

But this hidden powerhouse had already figured out a way to attack the “Cultivation Chat System” and was even implementing it.

Unfortunately... the entity’s attempt failed as soon as it began.

The “Cultivation Chat System” was far more unique than anticipated!

So unique, it was impossible to take over!

The system was an extension of Song Shuhang’s very existence, tied to his “Path of Immortality,” making it one of a kind.

As long as Song Shuhang existed, so would the “Cultivation Chat System.” If Song Shuhang perished, so would the system.

Moreover, behind the “Cultivation Chat System” stood Lady Long Luo, who served as the ultimate shield. Without breaking through Lady Long Luo’s defenses, the entity couldn’t even touch the system, let alone influence it.

To seize the “Cultivation Chat System,” one would first have to seize its root—Song Shuhang.

Only by capturing Song Shuhang could they claim the “Cultivation Chat System.”

After failing, the terrifying entity swiftly erased all traces of its actions... then deleted its account!

Using a method Song Shuhang was quite familiar with the “Heavenly Dao Black Room” technique of erasing all roots.

The erasure was confined to the “Cultivation Chat System.”

This impressive and flawless operation even made Lady Long Luo’s scalp tingle.

After erasing all traces, the entity disappeared without a trace.

It was as if nothing had ever happened.

Flawless. No evidence left behind.

However...

There are always things in this world that defy expectations.

When the resurrection ability of the “Immortal Fat Whale Golden Core” kicked in and Song Shuhang was reborn on the “Heavenly Emperor’s Throne Two,” the missing data in the “Cultivation Chat System” was also restored.

The only data ever missing in the “Cultivation Chat System” was the account of that terrifying entity behind the scenes.

So... after the entity deleted its account and left, a gray ID quietly resurrected in Song Shuhang’s “Cultivation Chat System.”

“Heh heh heh,” Song Shuhang chuckled.

The resurrected gray ID was now in “offline” status but still tightly connected to the terrifying entity behind the scenes.

“But now’s not the time,” Song Shuhang murmured softly.

Rushing to confront that terrifying entity now would only alert it.

Song Shuhang shifted his focus away from that gray ID, avoiding it so that the entity wouldn’t sense anything and become suspicious.

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

The top-tier powerhouses across all realms had an uncanny ability to hear even the faintest whispers—Song Shuhang had experienced this firsthand many times.

For instance, if he were to badmouth Father Goudan or mention Goudan in a negative light, the retribution from Father Goudan would soon follow. And then there was Senior White Two...

The same went for the Devil Emperor. Even when gravely injured, if Song Shuhang so much as muttered something bad about him behind his back, the Devil Emperor would sense it, perform a quick divination, and immediately track Song Shuhang down!

The supreme beings of all realms were just that powerful! So, if you wanted to plot against them, the first step was to find a way to block their celestial senses.

Of course, these beings didn’t just pick up on everything indiscriminately.

Certain conditions had to be met for them to sense anything at all. Factors like the level of threat, the closeness of the relationship, whether there was a conspiracy at play, whether it posed any danger to them, or if there were any information-blocking techniques involved—these all served as prerequisites. After a complex set of calculations, the supreme beings would then pick up on the situation.

They were busy, after all. They couldn’t be receiving alerts all day, like “ding-dong~ ding-dong~.”

Song Shuhang and the likes of Father Goudan, Goudan, Senior White Two, and Three-Eyed Senior had close connections, so just thinking about them would trigger their senses.

As for the Devil Emperor, since Song Shuhang was considered a “source of danger,” the moment he mentioned the Devil Emperor, the latter would instantly become agitated.

So...

Song Shuhang averted his gaze, pretending the restored gray ID didn’t exist and deliberately avoided focusing on it.

Otherwise, just having the thought of calculating against it, coupled with his current “threat level,” would trigger the opponent’s senses. They would then take a series of defensive measures, creating unnecessary trouble.

Currently, the “restored” gray ID’s connection to the supreme being was one-way, like it was sealed. There was no need to worry about the opponent using this ID to log back in and cause trouble.

As long as Song Shuhang didn’t intentionally activate this ID, it would remain as if it didn’t exist.

“I need to wait... at least until my Causality Saber can rub shoulders with a few more powerhouses,” Song Shuhang thought to himself.

One day, when I collect a complete set of ‘Divine Cards’ for my Causality Saber, nothing will be able to stand in my way—be it gods, Buddhas, demons, or anything else!

After a moment of quiet, passionate contemplation, Song Shuhang’s mood finally calmed down.

In the hazy mist, he shifted his position to the right, moving a couple of seats over to lean against the right armrest.

“It’s huge,” Song Shuhang remarked.

Like the dragon throne from ancient China, the Heavenly Emperor’s throne of the ancient Heavenly Court was particularly spacious. Sitting on one side of the armrest, one couldn’t even touch the other side.

But bigger isn’t always better... For example, now that Song Shuhang wanted to change his sitting position, he had to scoot over several seats, which was tiring.

“The Heavenly Emperor must have had terrible lower back problems,” Song Shuhang commented.

After saying this, he intentionally fell silent for a long while.

But the sound he expected—a voice with a ‘da’ ending—never came.

“Not even a reaction to a comment about a herniated disc? Or is it that she really hasn’t revived yet?” Song Shuhang mused, leaning against the right armrest.

Normally, when the ‘Immortal Whale Golden Core’ resurrection ability was activated, he should have revived on the spot. Where he fell, he should have risen again!

However, instead of reviving on the spot, he reappeared a long distance away, sitting on the ‘Heavenly Emperor’s Throne Two’ in the Heavenly Emperor’s palace!

This strange occurrence made Song Shuhang suspicious.

Could it be that the Heavenly Emperor was manipulating things behind the scenes?

Has she already revived?

Or is she using my ‘revival’ to secretly set up a scheme?

To be honest, the Heavenly Emperor had helped Song Shuhang a lot in the later stages.

She had been deliberately trying to befriend Song Shuhang.

Given her methods and experience, winning someone’s favor was easy for her—after all, she once gathered a large group of diverse and powerful cultivators around her, establishing the ancient Heavenly Court with herself at the center!

Her charisma was undeniable!

Over time, as Song Shuhang interacted with her, he found himself harboring less and less resentment toward her. This was a testament to her exceptional social skills.

Now, Song Shuhang only retained a baseline level of wariness toward her.

This cautious stance would remain unless there was a dramatic change in their relationship.

“Not coming out? Given the time, you should have already revived by now, right?” Song Shuhang, realizing he couldn’t provoke her, decided to cut to the chase.

His voice echoed through the ‘Heavenly Emperor’s Palace.’

But the Heavenly Emperor still didn’t respond.

Song Shuhang then opened the ‘Cultivation Chat’ system to check on the Heavenly Emperor’s status.

[Fox Friend] Heavenly Emperor  Dadadazi (Status: Deader than dead).

“So, dealing with you ‘deader than dead’ folks is really frustrating. Can’t everyone just be a bit more straightforward? Like me! People should trust each other more!” Song Shuhang sighed.

Just as he finished speaking, his own profile popped up in the ‘Cultivation Chat’ system.

[Server  Goudan  Group Leader] Song Shuhang (Status: Deader than dead).

Song Shuhang was speechless.

He was speechless.

He looked up at the sky.

Who would’ve thought... I’m also ‘deader than dead’ now.

But my soul is still intact, right? If my soul isn’t dead, how can I be ‘deader than dead’?

Could it be that my soul, which has been divided into 15+1 pieces, is also considered in a ‘dismembered’ state?

While Song Shuhang was deep in thought...

A rumbling sound came from the Heavenly Court fragment area within the core world—a sign that something massive had just landed. It was the sound of the Golden Trigram Island Lord moving his ‘Heavenly Court fragments’ over.

This time, the core assistant didn’t take the opportunity to forcefully expand the core world’s territory using the ‘Heavenly Court fragments’... after all, the Golden Trigram Island Lord’s ‘Heavenly Court fragments’ were only on loan. Once he was done, they’d be returned.

Rumble rumble~

With the Golden Trigram Island Lord’s ‘Heavenly Court fragments’ in place, the Heavenly Court fragment area within the core world began to resonate.

This resonance traveled across the ‘core world,’ reached the present world, and extended to most of the heavens and realms near the present world, including Earth!

This resonance signaled that the ‘ancient Heavenly Court fragments’ had reached a critical mass, and the basic framework of the ancient Heavenly Court had been rebuilt—announcing the rebirth of the ancient Heavenly Court that had fallen in ancient times!

This resonance had an effect similar to that of a ‘Saintly Sermon.’

In more than half of the heavens and realms, cultivators all looked up at the sky in the same direction.

In their sight, a magnificent palace’s phantom image appeared, floating above the clouds.

The Heavenly Court!

The invincible Heavenly Court had returned!

Chapter 2942: Heavens, who attracted the Heavenly Tribulation?

The ancient Heavenly City was similar. Cultivators of the Fifth Stage Realm and above could see the “Heavenly City” above the clouds as long as they raised their heads.

To the cultivators of that era, the only difference between the Heavenly Emperor and the Scholarly Sage was that the Heavenly Dao still existed in the era when the Heavenly Emperor lived. The Heavenly Emperor had never had the chance to defeat the significant figures of the myriad worlds.

What he said made sense.

In the Inner World.

The fragments of the Heavenly City were arranged according to the original layout of the Heavenly City.

“Who am I here to see?” The man pinched his chin.

A part of his existence and the path to immortality had been bitten off!

Master’s strength made Daozi feel proud... and pained.

The pain was indescribable.

For a moment, he seemed to be able to understand why the ‘Heavenly Dao Fat Ball’ hated the scholarly faction so much... This pain was simply engraved in his bones. He could not forget it even if he wanted to.

Cold sweat poured out of Daozi’s forehead like rain, dripping onto the fragment of the Heavenly City below.

His path to immortality, a part of his existence, had been bitten off by the ‘Code of Confucianism,’ and then stored inside it.

The Daozi’s realm and aura fell rapidly.

He was about to fall from the Immortal Realm back to the Tribulation Transcender Realm.

A ghost spirit was attracted by Daozi’s body and stepped out.

This was Daozi’s ghost spirit, and it had already been nurtured to maturity. It looked exactly the same as Daozi’s ghost spirit. This ghost spirit

had been found recently, and after signing a contract with Daozi, he had used the methods of an Immortal to rapidly ripen it.

This ghost spirit was also part of the plan.

This was also the reason why she wanted Daozi to cut off his path to immortality first.

Next, Daozi was going to inherit the ‘Dao of the Heavenly Emperor,’ the seat of the Heavenly Emperor.

The reason why Gold Trigram had entered the space similar to the Wielder’s small black room was to temporarily block the source of the attack.

In this way, the Daozi who inherited the position of the Heavenly Dao would become the only Heavenly Emperor in the myriad worlds and meet the standards of the ceremony later.

A few breaths later...

“Success!” The golden Cheng Lin took a step back weakly.

At the same time, a golden space opened behind her.

In the golden space stood a large number of heavenly soldiers and generals, as well as a few statues of Immortals who had yet to be freed, and an ice-cold Great Northern Emperor.

The Great Northern Emperor in the golden space was the Great Northern Emperor, but not the Great Northern Emperor.

He was the Great Northern Emperor’s mark that had once been left in the ancient Heavenly City. He had used Cheng Lin’s secret technique to transform... In fact, this was the ‘replacement’ for the 8.5 Wielder of the Will’s plan.

It was also because of Song Shuhang and Senior White... Pathfinder!

Chapter 2945: Someone Ascends to Immortality!

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

The long “loading screen” for resurrection finally ended.

Core World – Heavenly Court Fragment Area.

Now, Su Clan’s Sixteen had just completed the final stroke of her “Golden Core Composition.”

Her Golden Core Composition consisted of 108 images of herself, arranged in a pattern corresponding to the 108 heavenly stars.

These 108 Su Clan’s Sixteen images formed a “dragon” procession, resembling a New Year’s “dragon dance.”

And the last stroke for her Fifth-to-Sixth Stage Golden Core Composition depicted the eyes of this dragon.

This was a true “dotting the eyes” moment.

However, these “dragon eyes” were quite unusual.

This wave of heavenly tribulation was indeed no threat to her.

Another genius, with potential no less than the 13 Tribulation Immortals of the Confucian Sect.

The power of merit is vital for cultivators, as evident in Tyrant Song!

Nor did it disrupt the resonance between the “Heavenly Emperor’s Dao” within him and the throne.
