Chapter 2946: I’m Still Green, But He’s More Seasoned!

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

No matter what the issue is, it’s always safe to assume it’s related to Tyrannical Song.

Don’t ask why. Just know it’s always Tyrannical Song!

Nowadays, in the eyes of cultivators across all worlds, Tyrannical Song indeed has the bearing of someone who can suppress an entire era.

Tyrannical Song’s clone has been challenging top experts in the solar system, particularly on Mars, defeating them one after another without suffering a single loss!

Meanwhile, his true body even managed to slay the “Invincible Heavenly Emperor” from the previous era!

Tyrannical Song has also become the ruler of one of the myriad worlds, a “World Lord,” controlling an entire world.

And that’s not all...

It’s said that Tyrannical Song, as a mere “mortal,” even took control of the Nine Netherworlds, becoming its ruler!

Rumor has it that the previous Heavenly Dao was shattered because of him.

In the past six months, tales of Tyrannical Song have bombarded the minds of cultivators across the myriad worlds, spreading like wildfire.

While an Eighth Stage Profound Sage enjoys the “Everyone Knows You” buff due to the “Profound Sage Speech,” Tyrannical Song’s fame was earned through his fists. And let’s be honest, no one can match him in delivering the Profound Sage Speech either—he’s done it more times than anyone else! There’s simply no comparison.

In the “Cultivator Chat System,” countless cultivators have gathered in groups, discussing fervently.

“Is the one proving the Dao really Tyrannical Song?”

“But... Has Tyrannical Song already subdued all the ‘Immortals’ across the myriad worlds? Isn’t that a prerequisite for proving the Dao and attaining immortality—to suppress an era and become invincible?”

“But who would still challenge Tyrannical Song? It seems like no one, right?”

In the myriad worlds, everyone was speculating.

All eyes were on the skies, eagerly awaiting the revelation of who would prove the Dao and become the new Heavenly Dao.

—This year, cultivators across the myriad worlds have looked up to the skies at least once a month, sometimes several times a month, greatly alleviating spinal problems for low-level cultivators.

While there was much speculation among the general populace, the top-tier experts among the Immortals, the strongest of them all, understood that proving the Dao and becoming the Heavenly Dao wasn’t as easy as everyone imagined... but it wasn’t impossible either.

It’s both difficult and simple—a paradoxical situation.

Subduing the myriad worlds is indeed one condition for proving the Dao and becoming the Heavenly Dao. After all, if someone can truly overpower the myriad worlds, then their position as Heavenly Dao would be secure.

But in reality, not every Heavenly Dao throughout history accomplished the feat of subduing the myriad worlds—some of them didn’t even match the power of the Confucian Saints.

Although most Heavenly Daos had power comparable to the Confucian Saints before proving the Dao, the standards for proving the Dao seemed to differ in every era.

So perhaps it’s not always about “defeating everyone,” but rather fulfilling certain conditions and being recognized as worthy to prove the Dao and attain immortality!

Theoretically, any Immortal who has stepped onto their own path has the potential to prove the Dao and become the Heavenly Dao.

“Could Tyrannical Song have fulfilled some hidden condition?” speculated the top-tier experts.

...

In the Core World.

Golden Tranquil, along with the Ancient Heavenly Court’s Immortals and the Northern Emperor, seized the opportunity to retreat from the “Ancient Heavenly Court” region.

At the same time, Golden Tranquil extended her hand, using a gentle force to pull Su Clan’s Sixteen toward her, bringing her closer to the “Heavenly Court Fragment.”

Sixteen’s tribulation was still ongoing, and she couldn’t stray too far... Now was the time for her to receive the reward of the opportunity she had gained.

“Fellow Daoist Daozi, in the end, we’re entrusting our obsessions and our redemption to you!” Golden Tranquil said weakly.

Expending so many “substitutes” at once had nearly drained her.

“This is my chance at redemption too,” Daozi replied.

This was his only and final chance to save his junior brothers. Now that he had it, he wouldn’t let go.

Whoosh~

In the heavens, the rules of the previous Heavenly Dao began to operate. Like a rigid program, as long as the activation conditions were met, it would be triggered.

A pillar of light imbued with the aura of immortality descended from the sky, enveloping Daozi.

Daozi’s body was wrapped in immortal energy, beginning his transformation.

The undying and unending information flooded into his body, transforming his physical form and soul.

This scene was reflected in the myriad worlds.

Normally, when someone proves the Dao and ascends to Heavenly Dao, they can choose whether or not to reveal their identity, or even whether to broadcast their ascension to the myriad worlds.

But Daozi took a shortcut and wasn’t fully proving the Dao—he was merely becoming an interim 8.5th Heavenly Dao.

He had no control over this process.

So, his image began to be broadcast across the myriad worlds.

In that instant, cultivators across the myriad worlds saw a scholar in Confucian attire, sitting high on a golden throne.

Behind him was a phantom image of the “Ancient Heavenly Court.”

“It’s not Tyrannical Song?”

“Who is this scholar, a member of the Confucian School?”

“It’s Daozi, one of the Thirteen Tribulation Immortals of the Confucian School! But wasn’t he insane?”

“When did Daozi prove the Dao and become an Immortal?”

At that moment, the message boards across the myriad worlds exploded.

“Can he defeat Tyrannical Song?”

“The Thirteen Tribulation Immortals of the Confucian School are indeed powerful, and Daozi is the top disciple of the Confucian Saint... But he’s not the Confucian Saint himself. Why is it him who’s proving the Dao?”

This was completely unexpected.

No one had anticipated that it wouldn’t be Tyrannical Song proving the Dao, but rather Daozi, who had been much less prominent recently.

...

In the neighboring Heavenly Emperor Palace.

Song Shuhang, who was in a half-revived state, looked stunned.

He knew that Golden Tranquil, the Northern Emperor, Daoist Red Cloud, and Daozi—these top experts across the myriad worlds—would definitely create some major news event.

But he never expected the news to be this big, this explosive!

They actually managed to churn out a Heavenly Dao!

“Kneel to the big shots,” Song Shuhang muttered in awe.

After all, an elder is still an elder!

Even though he, Song Shuhang, had pulled off some wild moves, it was nothing compared to creating a “Nine Nether Ruler’s clone.”

Yet these big shots had directly gone and created an “Undying Heavenly Dao”!

This move deserves all the praise!

Song Shuhang quickly contacted the Northern Emperor: “Senior, you’re incredible...”

He was just about to shower the Northern Emperor and the other big shots with praise.

But just as he was about to start, the image of Daozi, projected across the myriad worlds and sitting high on the “Heavenly Emperor Throne,” suddenly changed.

Beside the majestic figure of Daozi, another figure appeared.

This figure hovered behind Daozi, like a ghost clinging to his back.

“Heavenly Emperor’s Child?” Song Shuhang’s first thought was this possibility.

But as soon as the thought crossed his mind, that ghostly figure became more solid.

The ghostly figure manifested, taking the shape of a young man.

The man had a gentle and kind expression, and just by looking at the lower half of his face, he seemed quite handsome.

“Isn’t that me?” Song Shuhang was bewildered.

Why was he appearing like a ghost, clinging to Senior Daozi’s back?

And the cultivators across the myriad worlds were in an uproar once again.

“It’s Tyrannical Song, it’s Tyrannical Song!”

“So Tyrannical Song was here all along. I knew it, how could it not be Tyrannical Song proving the Dao?”

“Even if it wasn’t Tyrannical Song directly, it had to be something related to him!”

“This is the correct way to go about it.”

Don’t ask why. Just know it’s always Tyrannical Song!

“Wait, that’s not me,” Song Shuhang muttered as he closely observed the ghostly figure hovering behind Daozi—he realized that this ghostly version of himself looked older!

Chapter 2947: The Whisper of the Old Overlord Song

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

Song Shuhang’s reference to “old” doesn’t pertain to any physical differences, but rather to the distinction in aura and temperament.

Take his current self, for instance. Although he doesn’t look physically older compared to last year, the overwhelming challenges and life-altering experiences he’s encountered over the past year have made him seem more weathered and mature.

Even if his appearance hasn’t changed, his aura makes him seem much “older.”

The “Ghost Song Shuhang” behind Daozi shared this characteristic—while he looked very similar to Song Shuhang, his demeanor seemed noticeably more mature.

Even though the “Ghost Song Shuhang” floated behind Daozi like a cloak, his presence still exuded an unmistakable sense of maturity.

A truly mature man looks composed and seasoned no matter what he does.

“Shuhang, what did you do?” The Northern Emperor immediately contacted the still-reviving Song Shuhang, his tone urgent.

This 8.5th Heaven’s Path Plan is critical to him, too. Like Wooden Song, he has a dear friend he wants to save. Therefore, he hopes the 8.5th Heaven’s Path Plan will succeed without a hitch.

Moreover, the throne of the Heavenly Emperor that Daozi is sitting on is something he exchanged for, by sacrificing his pride, for a chance to use it. Now, the anomaly behind Daozi is clearly connected to the Heavenly Emperor’s throne.

If it weren’t for Song Shuhang’s well-known character, the Northern Emperor might have considered filing a complaint with the “Consumer Protection Association” against Overlord Song!

Song Shuhang quickly clarified: “It’s not me, Senior Northern Emperor. I have no idea how that ghost version of me appeared... But look closely; it’s not really me. He looks a bit older than me.”

The Northern Emperor fell silent for a moment before responding: “Even if he appears slightly older than you... can you honestly say he has no connection to you?”

Song Shuhang was left speechless.

The Northern Emperor had hit the nail on the head.

The truth is, even if this “Ghost Song Shuhang” looks older, his face and appearance are unmistakably similar.

If someone were to claim that this “Ghost Song Shuhang” has no connection to the real Song Shuhang—even Song Shuhang himself wouldn’t believe it!

Why else would this ghost take on his likeness if there was no connection?

Song Shuhang conducted a quick self-assessment.

At the moment, he was still in the “reviving” state.

His “Iron Clone” hadn’t fled.

His “Three Corpses Avatar” was still intact.

His “Song Youyou” remained in the Netherworld.

His “Overlord Corpse,” the avatar integrated with the “Heavenly Dao Remnant,” was still in the Evil Lotus World.

“Could it be my secret technique clone? The one that disappeared with Onion Maiden?” A sudden thought struck Song Shuhang.

Onion Maiden, Song Shuhang’s clone, Heart Demon Akasha Sword, and Nine-Repair Phoenix Saber had all vanished into a black hole during the “Heaven’s Path Little Black Room Tunnel Explosion.”

But afterward... the Nine-Repair Phoenix Saber returned to him, fully upgraded to the Eighth Stage. Onion Maiden, Heart Demon Akasha Sword, and his clone, however, never reappeared.

“But, no... My clone wasn’t a ghost.” Song Shuhang frowned.

As he pondered, the Northern Emperor asked again: “Do you have any ideas? Will your “Ghost Song” interfere with Daozi’s path to ascension?”

“Sorry, Senior Northern Emperor, but I’m just as clueless about this “Ghost Song.” I’ve checked all my clones and avatars, and they’re all in normal states. The one problematic clone isn’t even a ghost. As for the ghostly figure behind the Heavenly Emperor’s throne, I have no idea...”

“Wait, the Heavenly Emperor’s throne! What if “Ghost Song” is connected to the Heavenly Emperor’s Child? That throne belongs to her. Could the “Heaven’s Path Ceremony” have triggered her resurrection? And maybe I accidentally became her resurrection’s anchor point? That could explain the emergence of “Ghost Song”!” Song Shuhang speculated as a sudden realization dawned on him.

The Northern Emperor was left speechless.

“Also, could it be related to the Thirteen Tribulation Immortals of Confucianism? My first spirit ghost was borrowed by the Glazed Scholar, one of the Thirteen Tribulation Immortals, who is closely connected to Daozi.” Song Shuhang felt like his brain was suddenly flooded with ideas, each potential connection surfacing in rapid succession.

“Wait, maybe it’s also linked to the “Heavenly Dao Ball”? When it collapsed, one of my necrotic kidneys got sucked in.” Song Shuhang recalled yet another detail.

The Northern Emperor was speechless.

“Or maybe it’s because someone accessed my “Core World”? I’ve mentioned before that the Core World absorbs “Heavenly Court Dao.” Now, the Confucian Heavenly Court fragments and my own Heavenly Court fragments, which are in the Core World, have all had their “Heavenly Court Dao” absorbed... Perhaps that triggered some sort of mutation?” Song Shuhang frowned.

On the other end, after carefully considering everything, the Northern Emperor finally decided: “Let’s cut ties, Overlord Song!”

You’re like a walking “event core”; wherever you stand, chaos follows.

To avoid getting caught up in another major incident, the Northern Emperor felt it was best to sever ties with Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang: “...”

At the same time, in the void, within the “Heavenly Dao Projection,” Daozi remained seated on the Heavenly Emperor’s throne, steady as ever.

He turned his gaze toward the “Ghost Song Shuhang” floating behind him.

With the insight of someone on the brink of becoming the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, one look at the “Ghost Song” revealed much to Daozi.

“Everyone, don’t worry. The Ghost Song Shuhang behind me won’t interfere with our ascension plan.” Daozi’s voice echoed in the minds of the Northern Emperor, Song Shuhang, and the others.

With Daozi’s reassurance, the Northern Emperor, the Eight-Armed Ancient Demon from Beyond the Skies, and the Great Master of the Diamond Temple all breathed a sigh of relief.

In the projection.

The Ghost Song Shuhang transitioned from floating to standing behind Daozi.

Then, he leaned in close to Daozi’s ear, whispering something.

After listening to “Ghost Song’s” words, Daozi’s expression suddenly changed.

His gaze sharpened, sweeping across a corner of the void like a blade.

“I won’t let you ruin my plan. This is my last chance... my teacher’s final request! Anyone who tries to thwart my plan will die!” Daozi declared coldly.

His voice grew even icier, like the mechanical hum of a soulless machine.

Daozi’s obsession was with his fellow disciples.

No one could stand in the way of his last opportunity.

After his sweeping gaze, Daozi flipped his hand.

The Confucian Saint’s “Confucian Canon” was summoned forth.

The next moment, Daozi hefted the hefty “Confucian Canon” and without hesitation, hurled it toward the corner of the void he had locked onto.

The projection of the myriad worlds still maintained the illusion of “Daozi’s ascension.”

Daozi’s strike carried the force of an “about-to-be-immortal” existence—an attack on the cusp of becoming the Heavenly Dao!

With one strike, the void shattered, spiritual energy annihilated... Over a hundred destructive heavenly phenomena engulfed that corner of the void!

Chapter 2948: The New Year’s Event Hosted by Heaven and the Cultivation Chat System!

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

As the scene of Daozi launching his attack played out, it was broadcasted across all realms, causing a massive stir among cultivators everywhere.

In the void, the image of Daozi striking at a certain point made the cultivators feel as if the attack was coming directly at them. The massive “Confucian Classic” he wielded seemed like the iron fist of knowledge, ready to smash into their faces.

Weaker cultivators, faced with this terrifying sight, collapsed to the ground. Thankfully, it was just a broadcast—had it been real, mere collapse would have been the least of their worries.

However, the stronger cultivators with steadfast wills managed to withstand the pressure, keeping their gaze fixed on the broadcast. For them, enduring this challenge was a great trial, one that could significantly strengthen their Dao Heart.

At the same time, countless questions arose in their minds:

“What did Senior Ba Song whisper to Daozi that made him so suddenly enraged?”

“Who is Daozi attacking? Is there really someone foolish enough to challenge him at this time?”

—

Boom!

Daozi’s attack obliterated a portion of the void.

To the viewers, it seemed impossible that anything could survive such a devastating strike—it was simply too overwhelming. Not even the formidable strength displayed by Senior Ba Song earlier could compare to Daozi’s current might.

Yet, just as the void began to crumble, two figures emerged from the chaos.

Below, Song Shuhang’s eyes narrowed.

His gaze, as sharp as a polished blade, locked onto the two figures. He knew their “names” well.

The Void Sun Guardian and the Stellar Doomsayer.

Among these, the Stellar Doomsayer was composed of many individual entities, while the Void Sun Guardian appeared to be a powerful eternal being, fragmented into countless “Void Suns.” However, these fragments seemed to operate independently; even if one were destroyed, it wouldn’t affect the original body—a truly unique condition.

In the void, both the Stellar Doomsayer and Void Sun Guardian were in a pitiful state. They each had been holding what seemed to be a scroll or book, but Daozi’s sudden strike had reduced them to mere fragments.

The Void Sun Guardian’s book had been reduced to just a binding strip, while the Stellar Doomsayer only had a tattered page left. The cloaks they wore were also incinerated by Daozi’s attack—these cloaks and books had shielded them from complete annihilation.

But now, without those two books, surviving Daozi’s next move seemed futile. Those books were crucial tools for them to interfere with Daozi’s ascension. Without them, how could they possibly stop him?

They had considered fleeing, but before they could even act on the thought, Daozi had already made his move.

With a casual flick of his wrist, Daozi summoned a scroll-like artifact covered in complex test questions. The scroll materialized an endless sea of questions, deep and profound—an ocean of knowledge.

The vast question sea engulfed the Void Sun Guardian and the Stellar Doomsayer, sealing their movements and confining their souls within the unending questions. There was no escape unless they could answer every question in the sea within a short span of time.

This was the nightmare of all scholars! If you didn’t study hard enough, if you didn’t acquire sufficient knowledge, how could you even think of fighting?

The Void Sun Guardian was an extremely powerful eternal being—if it tried, it might actually solve all the questions in the sea given enough time.

But Daozi had no intention of giving them that time.

As the question sea sealed off their retreat, Daozi clenched his fist. Empowered by Heaven’s Will, his fist broke through the limitations of space and relentlessly pummeled the Void Sun Guardian and the Stellar Doomsayer!

Daozi’s fists struck at a speed of millions of punches per second, an onslaught so overwhelming that the exact number of blows landed was impossible to count.

Yet, despite the rapidity of his strikes, Daozi controlled his strength with precision. This wasn’t just an attack—it was a venting of his fury, expressed through countless blows.

Among the top-tier eternal beings witnessing this scene, some found old wounds—long healed—suddenly aching again. They had once been crushed like this by the Confucian Sage, but Daozi, with Heaven’s Will as his aid, was even more ruthless.

At least when the Confucian Sage threw a punch, he had to open a “space gate,” and his fist would come through from the other side.

But Daozi’s fists ignored the boundaries of space entirely. His fists could simultaneously appear anywhere across the realms, even manifesting in multiple places at once.

Each punch he threw carried the full weight of his rage.

If only he weren’t punching so fast, Daozi would have loved to add a verbal taunt with each punch for maximum effect—but even he couldn’t imagine shouting out millions of insults per second.

After a few seconds, Daozi withdrew his fists.

During that short span, he had delivered billions of punches!

With Heaven’s Will empowering him, his strength was perfectly controlled, ensuring every blow landed solely on his targets. Otherwise, the force of those billions of punches would have reduced an entire world to ashes.

The Void Sun Guardian and the Stellar Doomsayer, who had given Song Shuhang so much trouble earlier—causing him to explode once—were now nothing but ash, obliterated by Daozi’s relentless fists.

This end was far more agonizing than a swift death by a single punch.

“Pity... but no matter,” Daozi murmured as he lowered his fists.

The ghostly figure of Song Shuhang leaned in to whisper something in Daozi’s ear, causing his anger to subside slightly. He nodded faintly.

Together with the ghostly Song, Daozi ascended to a certain height before disappearing.

Immediately afterward, a notification rang out in the minds of cultivators across all realms, via their Cultivation Chat System:

[System Alert: As the new year begins, we wish all fellow cultivators across the realms a Happy New Year and good fortune.]

[To celebrate the new year, the Cultivation Chat System, in collaboration with Heaven, will host a ‘New Year’s Event’ across the realms.]

[During the event, any cultivator who can collect the heads of two Void Sun Guardians or Stellar Doomsayers will be eligible to exchange them for a super reward through the Cultivation Chat System.]

[Additionally, anyone who can provide information on the whereabouts of the Void Sun Guardian or Stellar Doomsayer can also exchange their findings for rewards, with the level of rewards varying based on the quantity and quality of the information.]

With Heaven joining forces with the Cultivation Chat System for the New Year’s event, the prestige of the occasion skyrocketed!

Chapter 2949: Unprecedented!

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

This is essentially the new Heavenly Dao endorsing the “Cultivation Chat System”!

With the Heavenly Dao personally endorsing it, no product across the myriad realms can boast such a privilege.

As the system’s prestige soared, the power ceiling for “Cultivation Chat System” users quietly began to rise.

Originally, some top-tier big shots across the myriad realms either were in deep seclusion and hadn’t downloaded the “Cultivation Chat System,” or felt that the system seemed too trivial. Even those who had downloaded it didn’t engage with it much, and some outright dismissed its minor features, uninterested in benefits like the “sermons.”

“Ba Song” and his “Cultivation Chat System” weren’t some universally beloved spiritual stones; it wasn’t possible to force everyone across the myriad realms to like it.

In fact, even if it were spiritual stones, there were still some big shots who could smile and say, “I’m not interested in spiritual stones.” So, it’s even less surprising that they would have little interest in the “Cultivation Chat System.”

But now, a new Immortal has proved their Dao!

This is the true headline event across the myriad realms—no event in the coming eras could be more explosive or significant than a big shot proving their Immortality!

So, even those top-tier big shots in deep seclusion were so shocked that they had no choice but to emerge from their closed-door cultivation.

“A new Heavenly Dao proved their Dao? I’ve only been in seclusion for a hundred years!”

“I just started a long-term seclusion! I’ve only been in for ten years, and the world’s changed this much?”

“A few months ago, while in seclusion, I vaguely sensed the collapse of the Heavenly Dao. So, I planned to stay in seclusion for another ten years, adjust to my best state, and then break through... Now, a new Heavenly Dao has already proved their Dao? Did I miss a lot?”

“[Have I only been in seclusion for three years? Could it be that I’ve entered a special state of enlightenment, and a single glance already spans millennia?”

These top-tier long-life cultivators who emerged from deep seclusion were utterly bewildered.

Some had been in seclusion for hundreds or thousands of years, while others had only been in for ten years, three years, or even just a single year.

Especially those who had only been in seclusion for one year—they were completely lost.

So much had happened in just one year.

Thus, even after just a year of seclusion, they had been left behind by the times, unable to keep up with the year’s information.

Upon emerging, they were bombarded with tons of information—sermons by Saints, among other things, all waiting for them to absorb.

But the sermons were secondary... The most important news was the explosive headline of a new Immortal proving their Dao and the collaboration between the new Immortal and something called the “Cultivation Chat System,” which was launching a “New Year Event” for cultivators across the myriad realms.

Due to the Heavenly Dao’s prestige, these top-tier big shots who had just emerged from seclusion couldn’t help but download the “Cultivation Chat System” and register accounts.

If the Heavenly Dao was endorsing something, that meant it was connected to the Heavenly Dao.

For those seeking to glimpse the ultimate secrets of Immortality, perhaps this “Cultivation Chat System” could serve as a path.

Similarly, those top-tier big shots who initially dismissed the “Cultivation Chat System” or downloaded it but didn’t use it much—or hadn’t downloaded it at all—immediately reopened or downloaded the system, clicking into it without hesitation, thanks to the Heavenly Dao’s endorsement.

And in this “New Year Event” hosted by the “Cultivation Chat System” across the myriad realms, the task of collecting two “Solar Guardians’ or Starfall Doom-bringers’ heads” was, in fact, aimed at this segment of top-tier big shots!

Whether it’s two Solar Guardian heads, two Starfall Doom-bringer heads, or one of each, all could be directly exchanged for rewards through the “Cultivation Chat System” with the Heavenly Dao!

The rewards that the Heavenly Dao could offer to these top-tier big shots were already quite clear—Heavenly Dao-level sermons, or perhaps the chance to slightly glimpse “Immortal Information” or “Pseudo-Immortal Information.”

After all, these big shots had already reached their limits in power, sitting at the forefront of the long-life cultivators, just a tier below superpowers like the “Confucian Saints” and the “Heavenly Court’s Emperor.”

With their current levels, it was nearly impossible for them to progress further... Perhaps only by touching the Heavenly Dao and Immortal Information could they advance further.

Meanwhile, the task to “Simply locate the tracks of the Solar Guardians or Starfall Doom-bringers” was targeted at the high-end combat forces of the myriad realms—Ninefold Tribulation Immortals, Eighth Realm Saints, and even some battle-hardened Seventh Realm Masters.

This segment of the high-end combat forces had various means to search for traces of Solar Guardians or Starfall Doom-bringers, but they lacked the power to fight them.

With the release of these two tasks, top-tier big shots and high-end combat forces across the myriad realms were all mobilized.

However, the “8.5th Heavenly Dao,” Daoko, was not yet satisfied. He decided to add another activity to the event—since it was a “New Year Event for Everyone,” ordinary cultivators couldn’t be left out, right?

After all, ordinary cultivators were the true foundation of the myriad realms!

So, using the “Heavenly Dao Authority” that he hadn’t fully mastered, the “Half Heavenly Dao” Daoko captured a specific piece of information.

[——Whoever can locate and capture or slay members of the “Sun Worship Sect” or “Starfall Cult” across the myriad realms can directly exchange them for New Year’s gifts with the Heavenly Dao through the “Cultivation Chat System”! The higher the rank and the greater the number of captured or slain members, the more abundant the gifts.]

[Note: Ten Bronze Gifts can be combined into a Silver Gift, ten Silver Gifts can be combined into a Gold Gift, and ten Gold Gifts can be combined into a Supreme Gift... Opening ten or a hundred Supreme Gifts in a row will yield even richer rewards!]

[Attachment: Comprehensive Information on the Sun Worship Sect and Starfall Cult.]

Clearly... these Sun Worship Sect and Starfall Cult members were related to the Solar Guardians and Starfall Doom-bringers.

The task released by the “8.5th Heavenly Dao” Daoko was a call to mobilize all the cultivators across the myriad realms to deal with their enemies.

Using the collective power of the people across the myriad realms, they would raise a tidal wave of unimaginable proportions!

This New Year Event would be a revelry of unprecedented magnitude, one never seen before and never to be seen again!

Universal celebration!

In the core world, within the Heavenly Emperor’s Palace.

Song Shuhang quietly observed the three tasks released by the “Cultivation Chat System.”

At this moment, he was certain—the “Ghost Song” attached to Senior Daoko’s side was none other than himself!

Launching a “New Year Event” to target the Solar Guardians and Starfall Doom-bringers had been part of his plan all along.

And the later additions of treasure chests, chest combinations, and the ten or hundred consecutive openings... were all reminiscent of the mobile games that once made his liver quiver.

“Is it the future me?” Song Shuhang wondered silently.

He didn’t have the ability to transcend time, like Future Child, and appear in his own past.

But he did have the strange “dream-walking” ability.

Was it the future me who dream-walked into Senior Daoko’s Dao-proving moment?

Chapter 2950: The Principle Behind Tyrannical Song’s Path to Immortality

Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

If this really is... my future self, visiting the present through a dream while Daozi is in the midst of proving the Dao, then what kind of experiences must my future self have gone through to become so weathered?

Though the face and appearance are the same, the “Ghost Song” attached to Daozi looks at least ten years older than the current me.

What could have happened that made him mature like that?

Aside from death, what else can make a man grow up? Is it marriage, having kids, family responsibilities, the cost of baby formula, mortgage payments, car loans, children’s education costs, financial pressure... or maybe even the thought of a daughter getting married? This thought popped into my mind.

Death, or rather the near-death state, can lead to maturity by forcing one to see things more clearly.

Besides death, a man matures for those reasons I just mentioned.

Of course, there are even more pessimistic and desperate reasons.

For example, heartbreak. Or the loss of a loved one...

However, “Ghost Song” just seems more mature, without any hint of deep sorrow on his face. This suggests he hasn’t experienced anything that tragic.

“Except for getting married and having kids... I don’t have to worry about family burdens, financial pressure, or car and house issues anymore,” I said to myself.

As for housing, I have the Core World. I’m set to become the biggest real estate mogul in the cultivation world—definitely not short on homes!

Financial pressure is there; right now, I’m the biggest pauper in the “Nine Provinces Number One Group.”

But with the “Cultivation Chat System” in place, my future financial stress should ease up.

As for what I owe Senior White, he’s not charging interest, so I can pay it back slowly. Eventually, I’ll be debt-free, so money shouldn’t be too much of a concern either.

And when it comes to my kids’ education, that’s the least of my worries. With the seniors in the “Nine Provinces Number One Group” and all my protective artifacts, my future children and even my little sister, who will be born in half a year, will start their education at the highest level across all heavens and worlds.

So... is it because my daughter got married?

Which daughter?

Li Yinzhu? Xiao Lingxiao? Or is it my future daughter who hasn’t been born yet?

As one of the top figures in the heavens and worlds, a “Three Corpses Severing Tribulation Immortal,” my mind operates at an unimaginable speed.

When a thought forms, it can instantly branch out and evolve into numerous scenarios. Each branch can develop into hundreds of complete storylines.

In terms of word count, each thought could extend to at least three million words.

I even managed to imagine what my daughter might look like in nearly three hundred different ways.

Just as I was getting carried away, imagining multiple scenarios where my daughters get married, the “Cultivation Chat System” sent me a flood of information.

This data was relayed through Daozi, the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, and it’s precious information related to [Death].

I have two clues regarding my “Path to Immortality.”

One is related to “Death,” a prototype I developed after countless encounters with powerful beings, dying, and reviving repeatedly.

The other is tied to the “Cultivation Chat System,” a path so complex that it’s terrifying—completely beyond the reach of any cultivator. I have no way to grasp or deduce this path.

So, I’ve only ever tried to deduce my own “Death Path.”

Initially, I thought my “Death Path” might be something like “Seizing a thread of life in the midst of nine deaths,” a path where one seeks life in the face of death.

Or it could overlap with Senior Skylark’s “Revival Path,” being a variant of the resurrection path.

But now, the data transmitted from Daozi doesn’t match either of these interpretations.

After analyzing the data, combined with the information from my own body, the “Death Path” I possess becomes clearer.

After careful analysis, I frown—this “Death Path” is extreme.

This path to immortality straddles the line between life and death... but it’s different from Pavilion Master Chu’s path of the “Cycle of Life and Death,” where withering and flourishing endlessly alternate.

This “Death Path” requires me to remain in a state where I’m dead but haven’t fully revived.

Neither alive nor dead.

Dead, but not completely.

Revived, but not fully.

“Is this like the ‘dead but can’t die any further’ state of Cheng Gou Dan and Emperor Son?” I pondered.

Cheng Gou Dan is the typical example of someone who’s “truly dead,” a state where his soul and body are annihilated, yet he can still walk, talk, and even provide external support to me.

The Emperor Son’s state is slightly weaker than Cheng Gou Dan’s. Although she’s marked as “dead and can’t die any further,” ever since her “death,” she hasn’t sent me her daily energy drip, nor has she spoken or appeared again.

Following this line of thought, I examined my own body.

Yes!

It’s this special state!

Dead, and on the verge of revival.

But the revival process is being suppressed—the cooldown timer is long, and I can’t fully revive.

Neither dead nor alive.

**But what’s the principle behind this “Death Path” leading to immortality?** I furrowed my brow.

An immortality path needs to make sense; it requires a logical foundation.

Whether it’s the Puppet Path, Cheng Lin’s Reincarnation Path, or Pavilion Master Chu’s “Withering and Flourishing Cycle,” where withering nourishes flourishing, and flourishing eventually withers—they all make sense as paths to eternal existence.

They are theoretically sound paths to immortality.

But what’s the logic behind this “Neither Alive Nor Dead” path?

Is it because this state is so unique, placing me in some “no-man’s land” between life and death, where death can’t claim me, and life can’t restrict me, that I can attain immortality?

“If this is really the principle, then this path to immortality has flaws... just like that genius from the Ink Sect’s Puppet Path—it loses certain characteristics and concepts of ‘life,’” I mused.

I may have lost the ability to reproduce... but I haven’t lost hope, I still have dreams.

If I lose the characteristics of “life” entirely, then I might be facing a hopeless situation, one that even the “Path of Life” can’t save me from.

So, if the principle behind this immortality path is “Neither Alive Nor Dead,” should I really walk this path?

I hesitated.

And why did Daozi send me the data to complete this “Path to Immortality”?

“Cheng Lin and the Heavenly Emperor seem to be deliberately maintaining this state too...”

Clues gathered in my mind.

My computational power as a Three Corpses Severing Tribulation Immortal focused like never before, running at overclocked speeds.

Every memory, every piece of data, every bit of information in my mind was poured into this computation.

“Wait... two different entities proving the Dao together.”

“What if... these two entities, one alive and one dead, could achieve immortality together?”

Does it have to be that both entities are alive to prove the Dao?

If one of them is dead, could there still be a loophole?
